[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-market-depth-shu-ju#ding-yue-can-shu)

订阅参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

contract\_code

string

true

合约代码 或 合约标识

永续:BTC-USDT（永续合约代码） ，交割：BTC-USDT-210625（交割合约代码） 或 BTC-USDT-CW（当周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季合约标识）

type

string

true

Depth 类型

(150档数据) step0, step1, step2, step3, step4, step5, step14, step15, step16, step17（合并深度1-5,14-17）,step0时，不合并深度;(20档数据) step6, step7, step8, step9, step10, step11, step12, step13, step18, step19（合并深度7-13,18-19）；step6时，不合并深度；

备注: 合并深度仅改变显示方式，不改变实际成交价格。 step16、step17、step18、step19仅供SHIB-USDT合约使用，暂不支持其他合约使用。 step1至step5, step14至step17是进行了深度合并后的150档深度数据，step7至step13, step18, step19是进行了深度合并后的20档深度数据，对应精度如下： 档位 Depth 类型 精度 150档 step0 不合并 150档 step16 0.0000001 150档 step17 0.000001 150档 step1 0.00001 150档 step2 0.0001 150档 step3 0.001 150档 step4 0.01 150档 step5 0.1 150档 step14 1 150档 step15 10 20档 step6 不合并 20档 step18 0.0000001 20档 step19 0.000001 20档 step7 0.00001 20档 step8 0.0001 20档 step9 0.001 20档 step10 0.01 20档 step11 0.1 20档 step12 1 20档 step13 10

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-market-depth-shu-ju#shu-ju-geng-xin)

# 批量撤单 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/trade/cancel\_batch\_orders

请求类型: POST

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 交易

限频: 每个account 3秒最多 144 次请求(交易接口3秒最多 72 次请求，查询接口3秒最多 72 次请求) (该account的所有币种和不同到期日的合约的所有私有接口共享该限制)

接口描述: 此接口用于批量撤销合约订单，最多可以撤销10个

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/pi-liang-che-dan#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/pi-liang-che-dan#qing-qiu-can-shu)

数据类型

是否必填

描述

String

true

Array of string

false

# 用户持仓量限制的查询 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/position/position\_limit

请求类型: POST

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 读取

限频: 每个account 3秒最多 144 次请求(交易接口3秒最多 72 次请求，查询接口3秒最多 72 次请求) (该account的所有币种和不同到期日的合约的所有私有接口共享该限制) 。

接口描述: 该接口仅支持全仓模式。 请求参数contract\_code支持交割合约代码，格式为BTC-USDT。 pair、contract\_type和contract\_code。 business\_type 在查询交割合约数据时为必填参数。且参数值要传：futures 或 all 。

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/chi-cang-lei/yong-hu-chi-cang-liang-xian-zhi-de-cha-xun#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

# 订阅成交变动数据 | 孙悟空

trade.$contract\_code

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 读取

限频: WebSocket私有订单成交推送接口(需要API KEY验签) 一个UID最多同时建立30个私有订单成交推送WS链接。该用户在一个品种(包含该品种的所有周期的合约)上，仅需要维持一个订单推送WS链接即可。 单个链接为50次/秒的请求，单个IP链接为100次/秒的请求。 注意: 订单推送WS的限频，跟用户RESTFUL私有接口的限频是分开的，相互不影响。

接口描述: 发生成交事件时，推送如下消息。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/si-you-pin-dao/ding-yue-cheng-jiao-bian-dong-shu-ju#ding-yue-di-zhi)

订阅地址

环境

地址

线上环境

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/notification

线上环境（aws客户首选）

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/notification

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/si-you-pin-dao/ding-yue-cheng-jiao-bian-dong-shu-ju#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

字段名称

类型

说明

op

string

必填;操作名称，sub 或 unsub;

cid

string

选填;Client 请求唯一 ID

topic

string

必填; trade

contract\_code

string

# 市价全平 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/trade/position

请求类型: POST

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 交易

限频: 每个account 3秒最多 144 次请求(交易接口3秒最多 72 次请求，查询接口3秒最多 72 次请求) (该account的所有币种和不同到期日的合约的所有私有接口共享该限制) 。

接口描述: 此接口用于市价卖出指定的持仓

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/shi-jia-quan-ping#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

线上环境（aws客户首选）

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/shi-jia-quan-ping#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

contract\_code

String

true

合约代码

margin\_mode

String

true

保证金模式

cross：全仓 ；

position\_side

String

true

仓位方向

持仓方向 买卖模式下默认值both， 开平仓模式下： long：多 ，short：空

client\_order\_id

String

false

用户自定义订单ID

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/shi-jia-quan-ping#xiang-ying-can-shu)

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

order\_id

String

true

订单ID\[全局唯一\]

client\_order\_id

用户自己的订单id

# 全部撤单 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/trade/cancel\_all\_orders

请求类型: POST

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 交易

限频: 每个account 3秒最多 144 次请求(交易接口3秒最多 72 次请求，查询接口3秒最多 72 次请求) (该account的所有币种和不同到期日的合约的所有私有接口共享该限制)

接口描述: 撤销当前全部的挂单（不含策略单）。

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/quan-bu-che-dan#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

# Ws 合约批量下单 | 孙悟空

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-jiao-yi/ws-he-yue-pi-liang-xia-dan#place_batch_orders)

place\_batch\_orders

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 交易

限频: 共享REST限频次数。

接口描述: 该接口仅支持websocket合约批量下单。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-jiao-yi/ws-he-yue-pi-liang-xia-dan#ding-yue-di-zhi)

订阅地址

环境

地址

线上环境

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/trade

线上环境（aws客户首选）

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/trade

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-jiao-yi/ws-he-yue-pi-liang-xia-dan#ding-yue-can-shu)

订阅参数

字段名称

类型

说明

op

string

必填;操作名称为 place\_batch\_orders;

cid

string

选填; 请求唯一 ID

data

array

批量下单的参数

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-jiao-yi/ws-he-yue-pi-liang-xia-dan#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

<data>

true

订单参数

contract\_code

String

true

合约代码

margin\_mode

String

true

保证金模式 cross：全仓 ；

position\_side

String

false

仓位方向

"long":多 "short":空 “both”:单向持仓，开平模式必填，买卖模式默认为both。

side

String

true

订单方向

buy:买 "sell":卖

type

String

true

订单类型；枚举

"market": 市价，"limit":限价, "post\_only":只做maker

price\_match

String

false

最优档位，和price互斥

opponent-对手价、"optimal\_5"：最优5档，"optimal\_10"：最优10档，"optimal\_20"：最优20档

time\_in\_force

String

false

枚举fok, ioc, gtc，非必填，默认是gtc

client\_order\_id

String

false

用户自定义订单ID

\[1-9223372036854775807\]

price

String

false

价格，仅当限价单的时候有效，市价无需输入。

volume

String

true

委托张数。

reduce\_only

Integer

false

只减仓 0-否，1-是

tp\_trigger\_price

String

false

止盈触发价格

tp\_order\_price

String

false

止盈委托价格（最优N档委托类型时无需填写价格）

tp\_type

String

false

止盈委托类型,不填默认为market；市价：market，限价：limit ，最优5档： optimal\_5，最优10档：optimal\_10，最优20档：optimal\_20

tp\_trigger\_price\_type

String

false

止盈价格触发类型，默认是最新价

"last":最新价，"mark"：标记价格

sl\_trigger\_price

String

false

止损触发价格

sl\_order\_price

String

false

止损委托价格（最优N档委托类型时无需填写价格）

sl\_type

String

false

止损委托类型,不填默认为market; 市价:market，限价：limit ，最优5档： optimal\_5，最优10档：optimal\_10，最优20档：optimal\_20

sl\_trigger\_price\_type

String

false

止损价格触发类型，默认是最新价

"last":最新价，"mark"：标记价格

price\_protect

boolean

false

价差保护，默认为false。仅当设置止盈/止损需要该参数。

false 或者 true

self\_match\_prevent

String

false

防自成交

cancel\_taker ：撤销taker单 cancel\_maker：撤销maker单 cancel\_both：撤销全部订单

默认为 cancel\_taker

<data>

false

cid

string

false

表示本次请求id

备注: 备注: position\_side持仓方向 单向持仓模式下此参数非必填 如果填写仅可以选择both；在双向持仓模式下必填，且仅可选择 long 或 short。 双向持仓模式下，side和position\_side需要进行组合 买入开多（side 填写 buy； position\_side 填写 long ） 卖出开空（side 填写 sell； position\_side 填写 short ） 卖出平多（side 填写 sell；position\_side 填写 long ） 买入平空（side 填写 buy； position\_side 填写 short ） 单向持仓模式下，多仓返回buy，空仓返回sell

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-jiao-yi/ws-he-yue-pi-liang-xia-dan#fan-hui-can-shu)

# 查询当前持仓 | 孙悟空

请求类型: GET

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 读取

限频: 每个account 3秒最多 144 次请求(交易接口3秒最多 72 次请求，查询接口3秒最多 72 次请求) (该account的所有币种和不同到期日的合约的所有私有接口共享该限制) 。

接口描述: 此接口用于查询当前用户持仓仓位的信息。

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/chi-cang-lei/cha-xun-dang-qian-chi-cang#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

# 订阅Market Depth增量数据 | 孙悟空

market.$contract\_code.depth.size\_${size}.high\_freq

是否验签: 否

接口权限: 读取

限频: 行情类的公开接口，比如：获取K线数据、获取聚合行情、市场行情、获取行情深度数据、获取溢价指数K线、获取实时预测资金费率k线，获取基差数据、获取市场最近成交记录： websocket：req请求，同一时刻最多请求50次；sub请求，无限制，服务器主动推送数据

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式 请求参数contract\_code支持交割合约代码，格式为BTC-USDT-210625；同时支持合约标识，格式为 BTC-USDT（永续）、BTC-USDT-CW（当周）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季）。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-market-depth-zeng-liang-shu-ju#ding-yue-di-zhi)

订阅地址

环境

地址

线上环境

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/market

线上环境（aws客户首选）

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/market

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-market-depth-zeng-liang-shu-ju#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

字段名称

类型

说明

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4289016733-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2iWuuWL6k6J1cpi9pALC%252Fuploads%252FxDI68iCUvnzVGxRNBK5l%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D402ac9b3-1eed-41bd-9b45-14b14545b794&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5c435c10&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-market-depth-zeng-liang-shu-ju#gui-ze-shuo-ming)

规则说明

订阅(sub)

取消订阅(unsub)

规则

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4289016733-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F2iWuuWL6k6J1cpi9pALC%252Fuploads%252FdxrH0DEuYPSi7HY0jF1n%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De8446d61-9d49-4d8a-8f5a-d694e21a8778&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=50819008&sv=2)

无数据

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-market-depth-zeng-liang-shu-ju#ding-yue-can-shu)

订阅参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

contract\_code

string

true

合约代码 或 合约标识

永续:BTC-USDT（永续合约代码） ，交割：BTC-USDT-210625（交割合约代码） 或 BTC-USDT-CW（当周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季合约标识）

size

string

true

档位数

20:表示20档不合并的深度，150:表示150档不合并的深度

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-market-depth-zeng-liang-shu-ju#shu-ju-geng-xin)

数据更新

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

ch

string

true

数据所属的 channel，格式： market.$contract\_code.depth.size\_${size}.high\_freq

ts

long

true

进入行情服务器系统时间点，单位：毫秒

<tick>

false

mrid

long

true

订单ID

id

long

true

tick ID

asks

object

true

卖盘,\[price(挂单价), vol(此价格挂单张数)\], 按price升序

bids

object

true

买盘,\[price(挂单价), vol(此价格挂单张数)\], 按price降序

ts

long

true

系统检测orderbook时间点，单位：毫秒

version

long

true

版本号

ch

string

true

数据所属的 channel，格式： market.$symbol.depth.size\_${size}.high\_freq

event

string

true

事件类型；"update":更新，表示推送买卖各20档或150档不合并深度的增量数据；"snapshot":快照值，表示推送买卖各20档或150档不合并深度的全量数据

</tick>

false

备注: 1、当"data\_type"为incremental时，首次推送的"event"为"snapshot"的数据，且当重新发送订阅请求时，首次返回都是"snapshot"的数据； 2、深度即可以按照合约周期订阅，也可以按照合约代码订阅，行情系统在进行数据计算时，需要更新对应类型的数据； 3、version（版本号），是自增的序号，每次增加1，不管是增量还是全量数据,每个连接是唯一的。多个websocket连接的version是可能不同的。 4、每30ms检查一次orderbook，如果有更新，则推送，如果没有更新，则不推送。 5、如果是增量数据，要自己维护好本地的orderbook bidsasks 数据。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-market-depth-zeng-liang-shu-ju#ding-yue-shi-li)

订阅示例

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-market-depth-zeng-liang-shu-ju#ding-yue-cheng-gong-shi-li)

订阅成功示例

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-market-depth-zeng-liang-shu-ju#shu-ju-geng-xin-shi-li)

数据更新示例

# 订阅(sub)指数K线数据 | 孙悟空

market.$contract\_code.index.$period

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 读取

限频: 行情类的公开接口，比如：获取K线数据、获取聚合行情、市场行情、获取行情深度数据、获取溢价指数K线、获取实时预测资金费率k线，获取基差数据、获取市场最近成交记录： websocket：req请求，同一时刻最多请求50次；sub请求，无限制，服务器主动推送数据

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-sub-zhi-shukxian-shu-ju#ding-yue-di-zhi)

订阅地址

环境

地址

线上环境

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/market

线上环境（aws客户首选）

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/market

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-sub-zhi-shukxian-shu-ju#qing-qiu-can-shu)

订阅参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

contract\_code

string

true

指数标识

支持大小写，"BTC-USDT","ETH-USDT"...

period

string

true

K线类型

仅支持小写,1min, 5min, 15min, 30min, 60min,4hour,1day, 1mon

备注: 当指数有变化时会推送; 指数无变化时会根据订阅的周期推送；

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-sub-zhi-shukxian-shu-ju#shu-ju-geng-xin)

数据更新

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

ch

string

false

数据所属的 channel，格式： market.$contract\_code.index.$period

ts

long

false

响应生成时间点，单位：毫秒

<tick>

object array

false

id

string

false

指数K线id,也就是K线时间戳，K线起始时间

vol

string

false

成交量张数为0

count

decimal

false

成交笔数为0

open

string

false

开盘指数价

close

string

false

收盘指数价

low

string

false

最低指数价

high

string

false

最高指数价

amount

string

false

数值为0

</tick>

false

# 订阅 KLine 数据 | 孙悟空

market.$contract\_code.kline.$period

是否验签: 否

接口权限: 读取

限频: 行情类的公开接口，比如：获取K线数据、获取聚合行情、市场行情、获取行情深度数据、获取溢价指数K线、获取实时预测资金费率k线，获取基差数据、获取市场最近成交记录： websocket：req请求，同一时刻最多请求50次；sub请求，无限制，服务器主动推送数据

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式 请求参数contract\_code支持交割合约代码，格式为BTC-USDT-210625；同时支持合约标识，格式为 BTC-USDT（永续）、BTC-USDT-CW（当周）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季）。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-kline-shu-ju#ding-yue-di-zhi)

订阅地址

环境

地址

线上环境

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/market

线上环境（aws客户首选）

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/market

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-kline-shu-ju#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

类型

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-kline-shu-ju#ding-yue-can-shu)

订阅参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

contract\_code

string

true

合约代码 或 合约标识

永续:BTC-USDT（永续合约代码） ，交割：BTC-USDT-210625（交割合约代码） 或 BTC-USDT-CW（当周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季合约标识）

period

string

true

K线周期

仅支持小写：1min, 5min, 15min, 30min, 1hour,4hour,1day, 1mon

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-kline-shu-ju#shu-ju-geng-xin)

数据更新

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

ch

string

true

请求参数

ts

long

true

响应生成时间点，单位：毫秒

<tick>

false

id

long

true

K线ID,也就是K线时间戳，K线起始时间

mrid

long

true

订单ID

vol

decimal

true

成交量张数。 值是买卖双边之和

count

decimal

true

成交笔数。 值是买卖双边之和

open

decimal

true

开盘价

close

decimal

true

收盘价,当K线为最晚的一根时，是最新成交价

low

decimal

true

最低价

high

decimal

true

最高价

amount

decimal

true

成交量(币), 即 sum(每一笔成交量(张) \* 单张合约面值/该笔成交价)。 值是买卖双边之和

trade\_turnover

decimal

true

成交额, 即sum（每一笔成交张数 \* 合约面值 \* 成交价格）。 值是买卖双边之和

</tick>

false

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-kline-shu-ju#ding-yue-shi-li)

    }

---

# 订阅 Trade Detail 数据 | 孙悟空

market.$contract\_code.trade.detail

是否验签: 否

接口权限: 读取

限频: 行情类的公开接口，比如：获取K线数据、获取聚合行情、市场行情、获取行情深度数据、获取溢价指数K线、获取实时预测资金费率k线，获取基差数据、获取市场最近成交记录： websocket：req请求，同一时刻最多请求50次；sub请求，无限制，服务器主动推送数据

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式 请求参数contract\_code支持交割合约代码，格式为BTC-USDT-210625；同时支持合约标识，格式为 BTC-USDT（永续）、BTC-USDT-CW（当周）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季）。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/gong-gong-pin-dao/ding-yue-trade-detail-shu-ju#ding-yue-di-zhi)

订阅地址

环境

地址

线上环境

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/market

线上环境（aws客户首选）

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/market

# 订阅撮合后的订单数据 | 孙悟空

match\_orders.$contract\_code

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 读取

限频: WebSocket私有订单成交推送接口(需要API KEY验签) 一个UID最多同时建立30个私有订单成交推送WS链接。该用户在一个品种(包含该品种的所有周期的合约)上，仅需要维持一个订单推送WS链接即可。 单个链接为50次/秒的请求，单个IP链接为100次/秒的请求。 注意: 订单推送WS的限频，跟用户RESTFUL私有接口的限频是分开的，相互不影响。

接口描述: 当订单发生下单、订单撤单、成交等事件时，从撮合里引擎面推送消息

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/si-you-pin-dao/ding-yue-cuo-he-hou-de-ding-dan-shu-ju#ding-yue-di-zhi)

订阅地址

环境

地址

线上环境

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/notification

线上环境（aws客户首选）

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/notification

# 下单 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/trade/order

请求类型: POST

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 交易

限频: 每个account 3秒最多 144 次请求(交易接口3秒最多 72 次请求，查询接口3秒最多 72 次请求) (该account的所有币种和不同到期日的合约的所有私有接口共享该限制) 。

接口描述: 此接口用户合约下单交易。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/xia-dan#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

线上环境（aws客户首选）

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/xia-dan#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

contract\_code

String

true

合约代码

margin\_mode

String

true

保证金模式 cross：全仓 ；

position\_side

String

false

仓位方向

"long":多 "short":空 “both”:单向持仓，开平模式必填，买卖模式默认为both。

side

String

true

订单方向

buy:买 "sell":卖

type

true

"market": 市价，"limit":限价, "post\_only":只做maker

price\_match

String

false

最优档位，和price互斥

opponent-对手价、opponent-对手价、"optimal\_5"：最优5档，"optimal\_10"：最优10档，"optimal\_20"：最优20档

false

用户自定义订单ID

\[1-9223372036854775807\]

String

false

tp\_trigger\_price\_type

String

false

"last":最新价，"mark"：标记价格

false

boolean

false

false 或者 true

false

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/xia-dan#xiang-ying-can-shu)

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

true

订单ID

client\_order\_id

String

false

用户下单时填写的客户端订单ID，没填则不返回

备注: 备注: position\_side持仓方向 单向持仓模式下此参数非必填 如果填写仅可以选择both；在双向持仓模式下必填，且仅可选择 long 或 short。 双向持仓模式下，side和position\_side需要进行组合 买入开多（side 填写 buy； position\_side 填写 long ） 卖出开空（side 填写 sell； position\_side 填写 short ） 卖出平多（side 填写 sell；position\_side 填写 long ） 买入平空（side 填写 buy； position\_side 填写 short ） 单向持仓模式下，多仓返回buy，空仓返回sell

# 批量下单 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/trade/batch\_orders

请求类型: POST

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 交易

限频: 每个account 3秒最多 144 次请求(交易接口3秒最多 72 次请求，查询接口3秒最多 72 次请求) (该account的所有币种和不同到期日的合约的所有私有接口共享该限制) 。

接口描述: 接口用户合约批量下单交易

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/pi-liang-xia-dan#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

线上环境（aws客户首选）

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

# 订阅账户变动数据 | 孙悟空

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/si-you-pin-dao/ding-yue-zhang-hu-bian-dong-shu-ju#account)

account

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 读取

限频: WebSocket私有订单成交推送接口(需要API KEY验签) 一个UID最多同时建立30个私有订单成交推送WS链接。该用户在一个品种(包含该品种的所有周期的合约)上，仅需要维持一个订单推送WS链接即可。 单个链接为50次/秒的请求，单个IP链接为100次/秒的请求。 注意: 订单推送WS的限频，跟用户RESTFUL私有接口的限频是分开的，相互不影响。

接口描述: 当账户的静态金额发生变化的时刻(冻结、释放保证金、资金费率结算、已实现盈亏等)，推送如下账户相关信息

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/si-you-pin-dao/ding-yue-zhang-hu-bian-dong-shu-ju#ding-yue-di-zhi)

订阅地址

环境

地址

线上环境

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/notification

线上环境（aws客户首选）

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/notification

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/si-you-pin-dao/ding-yue-zhang-hu-bian-dong-shu-ju#qing-qiu-can-shu)

类型

说明

string

必填;操作名称，sub 或 unsub;

string

选填;Client 请求唯一 ID

string

必填;account

规则说明

账户变化通知相关事件说明

事件类型 snapshot：首推快照 create\_order: 订单下单 cancel\_order: 订单撤单 delivered：交割 transferred：划转 filled：成交 liquidation：强平 adl：ADL自动减仓 funding\_fee：资金费 set\_leverage：设置杠杆 price\_update ：价格更新 （api 用户不要） auto\_exchange：自动兑换

String

true

用户uid

<data>

true

state

String

true

账户状态

1(NORMAL):正常（交易，划转）、2(LOCKED):-暂时未用到、3(LIQUIDATING)：强平中，不允许交易、划转、收取资金费、4(BANKRUPTCY):暂时未用到 5(ADL):adl中，不允许交易、收取资金费、划转、6(OPEN\_LIMIT):风控撤单中，合约交易只允许下减仓单，可以转入，不允许转出

# 订阅持仓变动数据 | 孙悟空

positions.$contract\_code

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 读取

限频: WebSocket私有订单成交推送接口(需要API KEY验签) 一个UID最多同时建立30个私有订单成交推送WS链接。该用户在一个品种(包含该品种的所有周期的合约)上，仅需要维持一个订单推送WS链接即可。 单个链接为50次/秒的请求，单个IP链接为100次/秒的请求。 注意: 订单推送WS的限频，跟用户RESTFUL私有接口的限频是分开的，相互不影响。

接口描述: 当持仓信息发生变更时，例如形成仓位、加仓、平仓、逐仓增加/减少保证金等事件时,推送如下信息

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/si-you-pin-dao/ding-yue-chi-cang-bian-dong-shu-ju#ding-yue-di-zhi)

订阅地址

环境

地址

线上环境

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/notification

线上环境（aws客户首选）

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/notification

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/si-you-pin-dao/ding-yue-chi-cang-bian-dong-shu-ju#qing-qiu-can-shu)

# 获取聚合行情 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/market/detail/merged

请求类型: GET

是否验签: 否

接口权限: 读取

限频: 行情类的公开接口，比如：获取K线数据、获取聚合行情、市场行情、获取行情深度数据、获取溢价指数K线、获取实时预测资金费率k线，获取基差数据、获取市场最近成交记录： （1） restful接口：同一个IP, 所有业务（交割合约、币本位永续合约和U本位合约）总共1秒最多800个请求

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式 请求参数contract\_code支持交割合约代码，格式为BTC-USDT-210625；同时支持合约标识，格式为 BTC-USDT（永续）、BTC-USDT-CW（当周）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季）。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-ju-he-hang-qing#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

线上环境（aws客户首选）

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-ju-he-hang-qing#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

contract\_code

string

true

合约代码 或 合约标识

永续："BTC-USDT" ... ，交割：“BTC-USDT-210625”... 或 BTC-USDT-CW（当周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季合约标识）

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-ju-he-hang-qing#xiang-ying-can-shu)

响应参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

ch

string

true

数据所属的 channel，格式： market.$contract\_code.detail.merged

status

string

true

请求处理结果

ok , "error"

<tick>

object

true

开盘价和收盘价（从当天零点(UTC+8)开始）

id

long

true

K线ID,也就是K线时间戳

amount

string

true

成交量(币), 即 (成交量(张) \* 单张合约面值)（最近24（当前时间-24小时）小时成交量币）。 值是买卖双边之和

ask

array

true

\[卖1价,卖1量(张)\]

bid

array

true

\[买1价,买1量(张)\]

open

string

true

开盘价

close

string

true

收盘价,当K线为最晚的一根时，是最新成交价

count

decimal

true

成交笔数（当前时间-24小时）小时成交笔数）。 值是买卖双边之和

high

string

true

最高价

low

string

true

最低价

vol

string

true

成交量（张）（最近24（当前时间-24小时）小时成交量张）。 值是买卖双边之和

trade\_turnover

string

true

成交额，即 sum（每一笔成交张数 \* 合约面值 \* 成交价格）（当前时间-24小时）小时成交额）。 值是买卖双边之和

ts

long

true

时间戳

</tick>

false

ts

long

true

响应生成时间点，单位：毫秒

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-ju-he-hang-qing#qing-qiu-shi-li)

请求示例

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-ju-he-hang-qing#xiang-ying-shi-li)

# 获取行情深度数据 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/market/depth

请求类型: GET

是否验签: 否

接口权限: 读取

限频: 行情类的公开接口，比如：获取K线数据、获取聚合行情、市场行情、获取行情深度数据、获取溢价指数K线、获取实时预测资金费率k线，获取基差数据、获取市场最近成交记录： （1） restful接口：同一个IP, 所有业务（交割合约、币本位永续合约和U本位合约）总共1秒最多800个请求

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式 请求参数contract\_code支持交割合约代码，格式为BTC-USDT-210625；同时支持合约标识，格式为 BTC-USDT（永续）、BTC-USDT-CW（当周）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季）。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-hang-qing-shen-du-shu-ju#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

线上环境（aws客户首选）

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-hang-qing-shen-du-shu-ju#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

contract\_code

string

false

合约代码 或 合约标识

永续："BTC-USDT" ... ，交割：“BTC-USDT-210625”... 或 BTC-USDT-CW（当周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季合约标识）

type

string

true

深度类型

(150档数据) step0, step1, step2, step3, step4, step5, step14, step15, step16, step17（合并深度1-5,14-17）；step0时，不合并深度, (20档数据) step6, step7, step8, step9, step10, step11, step12, step13, step18, step19（合并深度7-13,18-19）；step6时，不合并深度

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-hang-qing-shen-du-shu-ju#xiang-ying-can-shu)

true

响应生成时间点，单位：毫秒

备注: 合并深度仅改变显示方式，不改变实际成交价格。 step16、step17、step18、step19仅供SHIB-USDT合约使用，暂不支持其他合约使用。 step1至step5, step14至step17是进行了深度合并后的150档深度数据，step7至step13, step18, step19 是进行了深度合并后的20档深度数据，对应精度如下： Depth 类型 精度 step16、step18 0.0000001 step17、step19 0.000001 step1、step7 0.00001 step2、step8 0.0001 step3、step9 0.001 step4、step10 0.01 step5、step11 0.1 step14、step12 1 step15、step13 10

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-hang-qing-shen-du-shu-ju#qing-qiu-shi-li)

# 获取K线数据 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/market/history/kline

请求类型: GET

是否验签: 否

接口权限: 读取

限频: 行情类的公开接口，比如：获取K线数据、获取聚合行情、市场行情、获取行情深度数据、获取溢价指数K线、获取实时预测资金费率k线，获取基差数据、获取市场最近成交记录： （1） restful接口：同一个IP, 所有业务（交割合约、币本位永续合约和U本位合约）总共1秒最多800个请求

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式 请求参数contract\_code支持交割合约代码，格式为BTC-USDT-210625；同时支持合约标识，格式为 BTC-USDT（永续）、BTC-USDT-CW（当周）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季）。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qukxian-shu-ju#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

线上环境（aws客户首选）

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qukxian-shu-ju#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

contract\_code

string

true

合约代码 或 合约标识

永续："BTC-USDT" ... ，交割：“BTC-USDT-210625”... 或 BTC-USDT-CW（当周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季合约标识）

period

string

true

K线类型

1min, 5min, 15min, 30min, 60min,4hour,1day,1week,1mon

size

int

false

获取数量，默认150

\[1,2000\]

from

long

false

开始时间戳 10位 单位S

to

long

false

结束时间戳 10位 单位S

备注: 1、size与from&to 必填其一，若全不填则返回空数据。 2、如果填写from，也要填写to。最多可获取连续两年的数据。 3、如果size、from、to 均填写，会忽略from、to参数。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qukxian-shu-ju#xiang-ying-can-shu)

响应参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

ch

string

true

数据所属的 channel，格式： market.period

<data>

object array

true

id

long

true

K线ID,也就是K线时间戳，K线起始时间

vol

decimal

true

成交量(张)。 值是买卖双边之和

count

decimal

true

成交笔数。 值是买卖双边之和

open

decimal

true

开盘价

close

decimal

true

收盘价,当K线为最晚的一根时，是最新成交价

low

decimal

true

最低价

high

decimal

true

最高价

amount

decimal

true

成交量(币), 即 (成交量(张) \* 单张合约面值)。 值是买卖双边之和

trade\_turnover

decimal

true

成交额，即 sum（每一笔成交张数 \* 合约面值 \* 成交价格）。 值是买卖双边之和

</data>

false

status

string

true

请求处理结果

ok , "error"

ts

long

true

响应生成时间点，单位：毫秒

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qukxian-shu-ju#qing-qiu-shi-li)

请求示例

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qukxian-shu-ju#xiang-ying-shi-li)

[下一页获取聚合行情](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-ju-he-hang-qing)

# 获取市场最优挂单 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/market/bbo

请求类型: GET

是否验签: 否

接口权限: 读取

限频: 行情类的公开接口，比如：获取K线数据、获取聚合行情、市场行情、获取行情深度数据、获取溢价指数K线、获取实时预测资金费率k线，获取基差数据、获取市场最近成交记录： （1） restful接口：同一个IP, 所有业务（交割合约、币本位永续合约和U本位合约）总共1秒最多800个请求

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式 请求参数contract\_code支持交割合约代码，格式为BTC-USDT-210625；同时支持合约标识，格式为 BTC-USDT（永续）、BTC-USDT-CW（当周）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季）。 business\_type 在查询交割合约数据时为必填参数。且参数值要传：futures 或 all 。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-shi-chang-zui-you-gua-dan#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

# 获取标记价格的K线数据 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/index/market/history/linear\_swap\_mark\_price\_kline

请求类型: GET

是否验签: 否

接口权限: 读取

限频: 行情类的公开接口，比如：获取K线数据、获取聚合行情、市场行情、获取行情深度数据、获取溢价指数K线、获取实时预测资金费率k线，获取基差数据、获取市场最近成交记录： （1） restful接口：同一个IP, 所有业务（交割合约、币本位永续合约和U本位合约）总共1秒最多800个请求

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式。 请求参数contract\_code支持交割合约代码，格式为BTC-USDT-210625；同时支持合约标识，格式为 BTC-USDT（永续）、BTC-USDT-CW（当周）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季）。

# 获取市场最近成交记录 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/market/trade

请求类型: GET

是否验签: 否

接口权限: 读取

限频: 行情类的公开接口，比如：获取K线数据、获取聚合行情、市场行情、获取行情深度数据、获取溢价指数K线、获取实时预测资金费率k线，获取基差数据、获取市场最近成交记录： （1） restful接口：同一个IP, 所有业务（交割合约、币本位永续合约和U本位合约）总共1秒最多800个请求

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式 请求参数contract\_code支持交割合约代码，格式为BTC-USDT-210625；同时支持合约标识，格式为 BTC-USDT（永续）、BTC-USDT-CW（当周）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季）。 business\_type 在查询交割合约数据时为必填参数。且参数值要传：futures 或 all 。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-shi-chang-zui-jin-cheng-jiao-ji-lu#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

线上环境（aws客户首选）

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-shi-chang-zui-jin-cheng-jiao-ji-lu#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

contract\_code

string

false

合约代码 或 合约标识

永续："BTC-USDT" ... ，交割：“BTC-USDT-210625”... 或 BTC-USDT-CW（当周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周合约标识）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季合约标识）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季合约标识）

business\_type

string

false

业务类型，不填默认永续

futures：交割、swap：永续、all：全部

# 获取合约的溢价指数K线 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/index/market/history/linear\_swap\_premium\_index\_kline

请求类型: GET

是否验签: 否

接口权限: 读取

限频: 行情类的公开接口，比如：获取K线数据、获取聚合行情、市场行情、获取行情深度数据、获取溢价指数K线、获取实时预测资金费率k线，获取基差数据、获取市场最近成交记录： （1） restful接口：同一个IP, 所有业务（交割合约、币本位永续合约和U本位合约）总共1秒最多800个请求

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-he-yue-de-yi-jia-zhi-shukxian#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

线上环境（aws客户首选）

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-he-yue-de-yi-jia-zhi-shukxian#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求类型: GET

限频: 行情类的公开接口，比如：获取K线数据、获取聚合行情、市场行情、获取行情深度数据、获取溢价指数K线、获取实时预测资金费率k线，获取基差数据、获取市场最近成交记录： （1） restful接口：同一个IP, 所有业务（交割合约、币本位永续合约和U本位合约）总共1秒最多800个请求

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式 请求参数contract\_code支持交割合约代码，格式为BTC-USDT-210625；同时支持合约标识，格式为 BTC-USDT（永续）、BTC-USDT-CW（当周）、BTC-USDT-NW（次周）、BTC-USDT-CQ（当季）、BTC-USDT-NQ（次季）。

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/pi-liang-huo-qu-zui-jin-de-jiao-yi-ji-lu#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

# 查询用户当前的下单量限制 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/trade/order\_limit

请求类型: POST

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 读取

限频: 每个account 3秒最多 144 次请求(交易接口3秒最多 72 次请求，查询接口3秒最多 72 次请求) (该account的所有币种和不同到期日的合约的所有私有接口共享该限制) 。

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式 请求参数contract\_code支持交割合约代码，格式为BTC-USDT-210625。 pair、contract\_type和contract\_code同时填写，优先取contract\_code。 business\_type 在查询交割合约数据时为必填参数。且参数值要传：futures 或 all 。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/cha-xun-yong-hu-dang-qian-de-xia-dan-liang-xian-zhi#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

线上环境（aws客户首选）

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/cha-xun-yong-hu-dang-qian-de-xia-dan-liang-xian-zhi#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

contract\_code

string

false

合约代码

永续"BTC-USDT"... ，交割："BTC-USDT-220325"...

# 获取实时预测资金费率的K线数据 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/index/market/history/linear\_swap\_estimated\_rate\_kline

请求类型: GET

是否验签: 否

接口权限: 读取

限频: 行情类的公开接口，比如：获取K线数据、获取聚合行情、市场行情、获取行情深度数据、获取溢价指数K线、获取实时预测资金费率k线，获取基差数据、获取市场最近成交记录： （1） restful接口：同一个IP, 所有业务（交割合约、币本位永续合约和U本位合约）总共1秒最多800个请求

接口描述: 该接口支持全仓模式和逐仓模式

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/hang-qing-shu-ju/huo-qu-shi-shi-yu-ce-zi-jin-feildekxian-shu-ju#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

# 查询成交明细 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/trade/order/details

请求类型: GET

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 读取

限频: 每个account 3秒最多 144 次请求(交易接口3秒最多 72 次请求，查询接口3秒最多 72 次请求) (该account的所有币种和不同到期日的合约的所有私有接口共享该限制) 。

接口描述: 此接口用于查询合约进3天订单成交明细

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/cha-xun-cheng-jiao-ming-xi#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

线上环境（aws客户首选）

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/cha-xun-cheng-jiao-ming-xi#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

contract\_code

String

false

合约代码

order\_id

String

false

订单的订单 ID

start\_time

String

false

查询开始时间，UNIX时间戳，以毫秒为单位。

取值范围 \[((end-time) – 48h), (end-time)\] ，查询窗口最大为48小时，窗口平移范围为最近90天。 默认值 (now) – 48h

end\_time

String

false

查询结束时间，UNIX时间戳，以毫秒为单位。

取值范围 \[(present-90d), present\] ，查询窗口最大为48小时，窗口平移范围为最近90天。 默认值：now

from

Long

false

查询的起始id，默认从0开始

limit

Integer

false

分页页面大小，默认为10，最大为100。

direct

String

false

翻页方向，prev, next，默认next

# 订阅订单数据 | 孙悟空

orders.$contract\_code

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 读取

限频: WebSocket私有订单成交推送接口(需要API KEY验签) 一个UID最多同时建立30个私有订单成交推送WS链接。该用户在一个品种(包含该品种的所有周期的合约)上，仅需要维持一个订单推送WS链接即可。 单个链接为50次/秒的请求，单个IP链接为100次/秒的请求。 注意: 订单推送WS的限频，跟用户RESTFUL私有接口的限频是分开的，相互不影响。

接口描述: 当订单发生下单、订单撤单等事件时，推送消息。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/si-you-pin-dao/ding-yue-ding-dan-shu-ju#ding-yue-di-zhi)

订阅地址

环境

地址

线上环境

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/notification

线上环境（aws客户首选）

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/notification

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/si-you-pin-dao/ding-yue-ding-dan-shu-ju#qing-qiu-can-shu)

字段名称

类型

说明

string

必填;操作名称，sub 或 unsub;

string

选填;Client 请求唯一 ID

topic

string

必填; orders

contract\_code

string

必填; contract\_code \* 或者 BTC-USDT 或者 BTC-USDT-240909

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/websocket-ding-yue/si-you-pin-dao/ding-yue-ding-dan-shu-ju#gui-ze-shuo-ming)

规则说明

订阅(sub)

取消订阅(unsub)

规则

\*

\*

允许

\*

contract\_code

不允许

String

true

<data>

false

备注: 假设订单一次成交，且匹配了多个完全成交，则订单频道多次推送的状态都是“filled-完全成交“，但成交量可能小于下单量. 假设IOC订单部分成交剩余撤单，则订单频道多次推送的状态都是“partially\_canceled-部分被撤销“，但成交量 + 撤单量可能小于下单量. 建议： 成交量 + 撤单量 是否等于 下单量 来辅助判断是否为最后一次更新

# 查询订单信息 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/trade/order

请求类型: GET

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 读取

限频: 每个account 3秒最多 144 次请求(交易接口3秒最多 72 次请求，查询接口3秒最多 72 次请求) (该account的所有币种和不同到期日的合约的所有私有接口共享该限制) 。

接口描述: 此接口用于查询订单的信息。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/cha-xun-ding-dan-xin-xi#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

线上环境（aws客户首选）

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/cha-xun-ding-dan-xin-xi#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

String

true

合约代码(币对)

"BTC-USDT"...

margin\_mode

String

true

保证金模式 cross：全仓 ；

order\_id

String

false

订单id，order\_id和client\_order\_id必填写一个，若都填写了以order\_id为准

client\_order\_id

String

false

用户自定义订单ID

cancel\_reason

String

true

撤单原因

created\_time

String

true

订单创建时间, UTC时间戳(MS)

"Limit order cancelation by the client":"用户主动撤销普通限价订单","Order cancelation by system":"系统撤单","Market order circuit-breaker":"市价单熔断","Bankruptcy price of market order":"市价单破产价","Order cancelation due to no matching orders":"没有对手盘导致撤单"," Self trading prevention":"防自成交撤单","Number of maker orders matched with your taker orders exceeding limit":"成交笔数超过最大限制","Order cancelation due to API timeout":"API超时撤单"

updated\_time

String

true

订单更新时间, UTC时间戳(MS)

self\_match\_prevent

String

true

防自成交

cancel\_taker: 撤销taker单 cancel\_maker：撤销maker单 cancel\_both：撤销全部订单

备注: 下列行为，都属于"Order cancelation by system":"系统撤单"的范围。 FOK order cancelation-- fok撤单 IOC order cancelation-- ioc撤单 Order cancelation by the management system-- MGT撤单 Limit maker order cancelation--limit-maker撤单 Order cancelation due to API timeout–api超时撤单 Order cancelation due to forced liquidation--强平撤单 Order cancelation due to ADL--adl撤单 Order cancelation due to delivery futures expiration--交割合约到期

# 查询当前委托 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/trade/order/opens

请求类型: GET

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 读取

限频: 每个account 3秒最多 144 次请求(交易接口3秒最多 72 次请求，查询接口3秒最多 72 次请求) (该account的所有币种和不同到期日的合约的所有私有接口共享该限制) 。

接口描述: 此接口用于查询合约当前未成交的委托单，若全部为否，则全量查询用户所有挂单，并且根据创建时间由早到晚进行排序。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/cha-xun-dang-qian-wei-tuo#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

线上环境（aws客户首选）

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/cha-xun-dang-qian-wei-tuo#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

String

false

合约代码

String

false

保证金模式

cross：全仓

false

long

false

Integer

false

分页页面大小，默认为10，最大为100。

String

false

翻页方向，prev, next，默认next

# 查询历史委托 | 孙悟空

/sapi/v1/trade/order/history

请求类型: GET

是否验签: 是

接口权限: 读取

限频: 每个account 3秒最多 144 次请求(交易接口3秒最多 72 次请求，查询接口3秒最多 72 次请求) (该account的所有币种和不同到期日的合约的所有私有接口共享该限制) 。

接口描述: 此接口用于查询历史委托的合约订单。

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/cha-xun-li-shi-wei-tuo#qing-qiu-di-zhi)

请求地址

环境

地址

线上环境

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

线上环境（aws客户首选）

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/cha-xun-li-shi-wei-tuo#qing-qiu-can-shu)

请求参数

参数

数据类型

是否必填

描述

取值范围

默认值

contract\_code

String

true

合约代码，必填项，查询永续合约和交割合约时，需使用指定合约代码

“BTC-USDT” “BTC-USDT-251103”...

margin\_mode

String

true

保证金模式 cross：全仓 ；

states

String

false

订单状态

可以查多个状态，使用逗号分隔。“filled“:”已成交”, ”partially\_canceled”:””部分成交已撤销, “canceled“:”已撤销”

type

String

false

订单类型

"market": 市价，"limit":限价，"post\_only":只做maker单

price\_match

String

false

最优档位

最优档位,opponent-对手价、"optimal\_5"：最优5档，"optimal\_10"：最优10档，"optimal\_20"：最优20档

time\_in\_force

String

false

生效时间

start\_time

String

false

查询开始时间, 以数据按创建时间进行查询，UNIX时间戳，以毫秒为单位。

取值范围 \[((end-time) – 48h), (end-time)\] ，查询窗口最大为48小时，窗口平移范围为最近90天。 默认值 (now) – 48h

end\_time

String

false

查询结束时间, 以数据按创建时间进行查询，UNIX时间戳，以毫秒为单位。

取值范围 \[(present-90d), present\] ，查询窗口最大为48小时，窗口平移范围为最近90天。 默认值：now

from

Long

false

查询的起始id，默认从0开始

limit

Integer

false

分页页面大小，默认为10，最大为100。

direct

String

false

翻页方向

prev, next，默认next

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx-cn/kai-fa-zhe/rest/ding-dan-lei/cha-xun-li-shi-wei-tuo#xiang-ying-can-shu)

contract\_type

String

true

合约类型

swap（永续）、this\_week（当周）、next\_week（次周）、quarter（当季）、next\_quarter（次季）

cancel\_reason

String

true

撤单原因

"Limit order cancelation by the client":"用户主动撤销普通限价订单","Order cancelation by system":"系统撤单","Market order circuit-breaker":"市价单熔断","Bankruptcy price of market order":"市价单破产价","Order cancelation due to no matching orders":"没有对手盘导致撤单"," Self trading prevention":"防自成交撤单","Number of maker orders matched with your taker orders exceeding limit":"成交笔数超过最大限制","Order cancelation due to API timeout":"API超时撤单"

created\_time

String

true

订单创建时间, UTC时间戳(MS)

updated\_time

String

true

订单更新时间, UTC时间戳(MS)

self\_match\_prevent

String

true

防自成交

cancel\_taker: 撤销taker单 cancel\_maker：撤销maker单 cancel\_both：撤销全部订单

备注: 下列行为，都属于"Order cancelation by system":"系统撤单"的范围。 FOK order cancelation-- fok撤单 IOC order cancelation-- ioc撤单 Order cancelation by the management system-- MGT撤单 Limit maker order cancelation--limit-maker撤单 Order cancelation due to API timeout–api超时撤单 Order cancelation due to forced liquidation--强平撤单 Order cancelation due to ADL--adl撤单 Order cancelation due to delivery futures expiration--交割合约到期

# Introduction | SunX

**About** SunX

SunX is the first top-tier decentralized perpetual contract trading platform on the TRON blockchain, dedicated to providing users with an institutional-grade trading experience and ultimate asset security. By deeply integrating cross-chain liquidity, gas-free transactions, and intelligent risk control mechanisms, we are redefining efficient, convenient, and reliable DeFi derivatives trading.

**Core Advantages**

**·** Deep Aggregated Liquidity: Seamlessly integrated with top multi-chain liquidity sources, supporting instant execution of large-volume trades with near-zero slippage, delivering a CEX-like smooth trading experience.

· High-Speed Trading Performance: Millisecond-order matching and high-performance APIs, combined with intelligent on-chain routing technology, ensure rapid response and seamless operation, so you never miss a market opportunity.

· Zero Gas Fee Structure: An innovative hybrid model of off-chain execution and on-chain settlement allows users to trade without paying gas fees, significantly reducing the cost of frequent trading.

· Multi-Layered Intelligent Risk Control: Innovative anti-snipe mechanisms and multi-source oracle real-time pricing effectively avoid unexpected risks caused by abnormal market fluctuations, safeguarding your funds throughout the entire process.

[NextAccounts & Wallets](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/accounts-and-wallets)

Last updated 28 days ago

# Accounts & Wallets | SunX

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/accounts-and-wallets#sunx-wallet-connection-guide)

SunX — Wallet Connection Guide


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide explains how to connect a wallet to SunX.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/accounts-and-wallets#at-a-glance)

At a Glance

1) Open SunX → 2) Click “Connect Wallet” → 3) Choose one of the supported wallets → 4) Sign the message → 5) You’re connected.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/accounts-and-wallets#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

\- Install one of the supported wallets (exact four options listed in the connect dialog). - Make sure the wallet extension/app is unlocked. - You do not need gas to connect; network fees apply only when you later submit on-chain transactions.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/accounts-and-wallets#connect-your-wallet)

Connect Your Wallet

1\. Open the official [SunX](https://www.sunperp.com/)
 app and locate the “Connect Wallet” button in the top-right header.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FmeAqWSYThjIiQjbCwmP5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db1d77e76-b4e1-486d-9727-6731965f2af0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bf322ebb&sv=2)

2\. Click “Connect Wallet”. A modal appears with exactly four wallet options as implemented by SunX:

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FYZwM5C3SGJiiQuNmLcTn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b480d98-1f0d-4f54-b769-d91124ee61a2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b71ba4a&sv=2)

3\. Select your wallet and follow the context-specific prompts:

• Browser Extension wallets (e.g., Tronlink): - Ensure the extension is enabled in your browser. - If prompted, approve the connection/authorization to SunX’s site. - A sign-in message will appear; review and sign to complete the connection.

• Mobile/Bridge-style wallets (e.g., if one of these options is a QR-based connector): - Click the option to display a QR code. - Open the wallet app on your phone and scan the QR. - Approve the connection in your mobile wallet, then sign the message.

4\. After signing, your wallet address will appear in the header. SunX does not require chain selection at this step.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FWuk74afp4szr3gMHZdZ3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dadc120bd-fc21-4f94-8e59-7480b1fb78b2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1ab699f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/accounts-and-wallets#about-the-sign-in-message)

About the Sign-In Message

SunX requests a one-time signature to verify wallet ownership and establish a session. This signature does not grant spending permissions and does not incur gas fees. Always read the message and confirm the domain before signing.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/accounts-and-wallets#verify-connection-and-switch-accounts)

Verify Connection & Switch Accounts

\- Once connected, your address is displayed in the header.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FerS0D071YUTzEx5FpUYf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcffc8867-ed67-4e0f-840b-7c437974342e&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=73703059&sv=2)

\- To switch accounts, change the active account inside your wallet and click “Disconnect” → “Connect Wallet” again.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252F43eJdWxJJ4AE85kAyX2r%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df53415d7-df48-462f-a2ee-594b4137c7ff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8b9dcaa9&sv=2)

\- If a signature prompt re-appears, sign again to refresh the session.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/accounts-and-wallets#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting

\- Wallet not detected: Confirm the correct extension is installed and enabled. Close other wallet extensions that might conflict. - Connect modal does not appear: Refresh the page and ensure pop-up blockers are disabled. - Signature fails: Unlock your wallet, check system time, and try again. If the issue persists, disconnect and reconnect your wallet. - Wrong account connected: Switch the active account in your wallet, then reconnect in SunX.

# Guide to Deposits and Withdrawals | SunX

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/guide-to-deposits-and-withdrawals#sunx-deposit-and-withdrawal-guide)

SunX — Deposit & Withdrawal Guide


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide explains how to deposit and withdraw funds on SunX.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/guide-to-deposits-and-withdrawals#deposit)

Deposit

Before you can start trading on SunX, you need to deposit supported tokens into the platform. Follow the steps below carefully to ensure a smooth process.

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/guide-to-deposits-and-withdrawals#step-1-connect-your-wallet)

Step 1: Connect Your Wallet

1\. Open the [SunX app](https://www.sunperp.com/)
 and click \[Connect Wallet\] in the top-right header.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252Fzau5kAx90cV9zsLYMqhn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddaf34afb-30e1-4a07-af1a-efd0dfd7af6e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f12e78cc&sv=2)

2\. Select one of all supported wallets and complete the connection flow. 3. Once connected, your wallet address will be displayed in the header.

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/guide-to-deposits-and-withdrawals#step-2-approve-usdt-first-time-only)

Step 2: Approve USDT (First-Time Only)

1\. If this is your first deposit of USDT, you must approve the token for use on SunX. 2. In the \[Deposit\] modal, click \[Approve USDT\]. A transaction request will appear in your wallet.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FdgfVtkpsjVky69WwqGYA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8573c11-f8fb-4fcb-a689-e951f8457392&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f898ef9e&sv=2)

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FO7FWBak3psygNgKwLWWR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De86d2896-54e5-452d-83f6-29e871e86b5a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cd96b9ad&sv=2)

3\. Carefully check the contract address before approving. The official SunX contract is: TEubMt2TNag5NN1JXVaeysUk8GNTTYmtVX 4. Confirm the approval transaction in your wallet.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FaDGgLC7bvSCZZdn608P1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d809dce-12bd-4d46-ad32-d76ee1a99341&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5ff63d80&sv=2) 5. Wait until the approval transaction is confirmed on-chain. Once confirmed, you can proceed with deposits. \_Note: If you have already granted sufficient USDT allowance to this contract, this step will be skipped automatically.

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/guide-to-deposits-and-withdrawals#step-3-deposit-funds)

Step 3: Deposit Funds

1\. After approval, return to the \[Deposit\] modal.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FMa1cAjqBx6JXiV8zvMj5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D27645f8c-bf1a-4999-a1d2-37ff09cad09a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=18f9039f&sv=2)

2\. Select the token (e.g., USDT) and enter the deposit amount. 3. Click \[Confirm Deposit\]. A transaction request will appear in your wallet.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FlUeI3mKIyIlbWf9dUOkn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d05f6e7-3e29-42e8-ab72-9d4cdd0ecbc4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7865828&sv=2)

4\. Review and sign the deposit transaction. 5. Wait for blockchain confirmation. Do not close or refresh the page during this step. 6. Once confirmed, your balance will be updated in the [\[Portfolio\]](https://www.sunperp.com/futures/portfolio/)
 page.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FQDOJyYEgEBurZKXle2b8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D445a2116-b635-4ea1-a268-ce36e6fc6e85&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=408b25ee&sv=2)

7\. You can review completed deposits in the \[Detail → Deposit History\] section.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FYFyYP8PaDbaC2EsN2AY1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db769e237-bf73-40f7-8040-b27a4e81cb19&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e0543bf5&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/guide-to-deposits-and-withdrawals#important-notes-for-deposits)

Important Notes for Deposits

\- Ensure you have enough native tokens in your wallet (e.g., TRX on TRON) to cover network gas fees. - Only approve the official contract address provided above. Approving unknown contracts may put your funds at risk. - Deposits are irreversible once confirmed on-chain. Always double-check token and amount before approving.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/guide-to-deposits-and-withdrawals#withdraw)

Withdraw

Withdrawals allow you to transfer funds from SunX back to your connected wallet.

1\. In the [SunX app](https://www.sunperp.com/)
, click the \[Withdraw\] button.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FfktsNc6JdROIzaZ1teFH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99e1d6c9-455e-4f73-9d7e-8434cb0c9d56&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e0697de&sv=2)

2\. Select the token and amount you wish to withdraw.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FLwHbCM4GVbQzkrnQ8g4j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D467377ae-23cb-4fd5-a90b-f269d1cd94e1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=32dcfbe8&sv=2)

3\. A transfer request will appear in your wallet. Review carefully and approve the transaction.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FTOO15uGogLAfV9ToZthk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D92792f93-f1a4-4329-a529-e2dddaf6f23b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d277f5a&sv=2)

4\. Wait for blockchain confirmation. The withdrawn amount will then appear in your wallet balance. 5. To review all past withdrawals, navigate to \[Detail → Withdrawal History\].

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FAGgeJBQTinb1q9fMv8rF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25380f78-9566-48f0-8f05-2c2eb93aa441&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=76c65848&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/guide-to-deposits-and-withdrawals#important-notes-for-withdrawals)

Important Notes for Withdrawals

\- Withdrawal requests that remain unconfirmed due to network congestion may require additional time.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/guide-to-deposits-and-withdrawals#sunx-platform-wide-withdrawal-limit)

SunX Platform-wide Withdrawal Limit

SunX enforces a single global withdrawal limit across the entire platform: - The maximum withdrawal amount for all users combined is capped at 2,000,000 USD per hour.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/guide-to-deposits-and-withdrawals#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting

\- Deposit not showing: Ensure your transaction has been confirmed on-chain. Refresh the page or check \[Deposit History\]. - Withdrawal delayed: Network congestion may extend confirmation times. Check blockchain explorer for status. - Insufficient gas: Ensure your wallet has enough native tokens for gas fees. - Wrong token sent: Depositing unsupported tokens may result in permanent loss.

# Auto-Deleveraging (ADL) | SunX

1\. What is ADL?

Auto-Deleveraging (ADL) is a mechanism of forcibly liquidating positions to minimize the traders and the platform's overall risk, in the event of depletion or rapid drawdown of the insurance fund due to extreme market conditions or force majeure. A rapid drawback refers to the insurance fund falling from its peak by a preset threshold within 1, 2, 4, or 8 hours. The exact thresholds vary by trading pair and may be adjusted by the platform in response to market conditions and user protection principles.

2\. How does ADL work?

When ADL is triggered, the system selects positions for deleveraging based on their priority ranking instead of liquidations through the order book. Thus, after the execution, the counterparty positions will be reduced, and the funds from the closed positions will be added to their account balances.

Please note ADL execution prices may deviate from the specific contract's real-time market price. We strongly recommend monitoring the ADL Indicator (priority level signal) to avoid being selected as a counterparty.

3\. How is ADL priority determined?

ADL uses a ranking system based on both account (or position) risk levels and position profitability.

\[Cross Margin Mode\]

· Profitable position: Leveraged PnL = Position PnL percentage / Account margin ratio

· Losing position: Leverage PnL = Position PnL percentage \* Account margin ratio

Accounts with a higher PnL percentage and a lower margin ratio are more likely to be placed higher in the ADL queue.

4\. Risk Reminder and Inquiry

You can track your ADL priority level via the indicator:

· 5 bars lit: You are at the top of the queue, indicating very high risk.

· 1 bar lit: You are at the bottom of the queue, indicating low risk.

If an ADL event occurs, you will receive an SMS and email notification, including details of the reduced position and execution price. You can also view this record on the Order History page, where the order type is labeled as ADL.

[PreviousSunX Online Q&A](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/entry-level/sunx-online-q-and-a)
[NextMark Price](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/mark-price)

Last updated 3 months ago

# SunX Online Q&A | SunX

SunX Online Q&A (Nov. 27, 2025)

**79、What are the eligibility requirements to claim rewards from the Airdrop for All event?**

Users who have registered on the Hyperliquid platform with an Arbitrum-chain address, connected it to SunX, and completed trades totaling at least 100 USDT are eligible to claim the airdrop reward.

**78、Regarding “zero-fee” trading in Trade to Earn, does that mean no fee is deducted?**

Trading fees are normally charged at the time of the transaction. However, when you claim your Trade to Earn rewards, you will receive a rebate of 107%–110% of the fees, effectively making it a zero-fee trade.

**77、Why do Maker orders get higher rewards in Trade to Earn?**

Since Maker orders provide liquidity to the platform, improving market depth and reducing slippage, SunX offers higher incentive rates — up to 110% — to reward this contribution.

**76、Will the fees collected from Trade to Earn be used to buy back and burn $SUN?**

Yes. The platform uses all collected fees to repurchase and burn $SUN. The amount repurchased daily will be publicly disclosed, and cumulative repurchase data can be viewed on the Trade to Earn page. The actual burn of repurchased tokens occurs quarterly.

**75、Do I need to register first before my trades count toward Trade to Earn?**

Yes. You must register for the Trade to Earn event first, and then trade BTC, ETH or SUN. As long as your trading volume reaches the requirement before the end of the event, you will receive the corresponding trading rewards.

SunX Online Q&A (Nov. 25, 2025)

**74、What is "Trade to Earn"?** "Trade to Earn" is a limited-time incentive event launched by SunX. When you trade the designated futures pairs during the event, you not only get a sweet 100% discount on trading fees but also earn extra SUN tokens. Basically, the more you trade, the more you get!

**73、How are "Trade to Earn" rewards calculated?** Reward = Trading fee × Weight factor. Makers get a weight factor of 110%, and Takers get 107%. So, if you pay 100 USDT in trading fee, a Maker order earns you 110 USDT worth of SUN tokens, and a Taker order gets you 107 USDT in SUN.

**72、Which cryptocurrencies are eligible for "Trade to Earn"?** Currently, you may trade BTCUSDT, ETHUSDT, or SUNUSDT to win rewards from the "Trade to Earn" event.

**71、How do I participate in "Trade to Earn"?** You just need to register for the event on the "Trade to Earn" page, and then start trading the designated pairs on SunX. Please note that the daily and hourly prize pools have caps. If a phase's prize pools are being completely claimed, you won't get any more rewards until the next phase. You can always check the prize pool progress on the event page.

**70、If I don't claim my USDT staking rewards for 2-3 days, will the earnings disappear?** Your earnings won't disappear! You may choose to claim them daily, or let them build up and collect them all at once after a few days. But, we actually recommend claiming daily. That way, your earnings can start compounding immediately, helping you maximize your yields!

SunPerp Online Q&A (Nov. 12, 2025)

**69、Why can't I see my previous trading history?**

Currently, SunPerp only supports viewing trading records from the last 30 days.

**68、I use an OKX Wallet. When I make approvals, do those fees go to OKX or to SunPerp?**

Approval is an on-chain transaction, so the related fees are collected by the corresponding public blockchain, not by the wallet service provider or SunPerp. For instance, if you use a TRON wallet, the fee is collected by the TRON network; if you use an Ethereum wallet, the fee is collected by the Ethereum network.

**67、If I use Energy for the first approval and make a deposit of 100 USDT, do I get a 10 TRX reward?**

If you complete your first approval using Energy and deposit 100 USDT or more, you will receive a reward of 3 TRX, not 10.

**66、I was charged a 10.36 TRX fee when I made a deposit. Who collected that fee?**

That specific charge is the fee required for the on-chain transaction, and it is collected directly by the TRON network. If you deposit 100 USDT or more after your first approval, SunPerp will rebate you 10 TRX.

**65、How do I withdraw funds from SunPerp?**

After connecting your wallet, simply click the Deposit button in the top right corner of our homepage. Once you enter that page, you can select Withdraw to continue.

SunX Online Q&A (Nov. 16, 2025)

**64\. I’m a beginner. Which wallet should I use to access** SunX **? Ideally, I’d like one that works on both mobile and desktop.**

If you are new to decentralized wallets, we recommend using TronLink, the official wallet of the TRON network. It offers the best compatibility and user experience. You can download it from tronlink.org, and it supports both mobile and desktop synchronization.

**63\. If I deposit using a non-TRON chain wallet address, how can I claim SUN tokens?**

Users who deposit via non-TRON chain wallets can still claim the SUN Welcome Bonus. However, since SUN tokens are currently not issued on other public blockchains, withdrawals to non-TRON wallets are not supported at this time. We are designing a cross-chain solution, so please stay tuned for future announcements.

**62\. Are referral rewards distributed automatically or do I need to claim them manually?**

Fee rebate rewards will be automatically distributed to your account on T+1 day, with no action required. However, referral rewards from the Welcome Campaign must be claimed manually on the “Welcome Fiesta” page.

**61\. Does** SunX **have its own TGE narrative?**

At present, the SunX platform has no plans to launch a new token (TGE). The platform’s official token remains $SUN.

**60\. Has the APY for USDT staking changed to 7%?**

As the platform’s total funds surpassed $77 million, the USDT staking APY has been adjusted to a tiered structure: The base yield is 7%; For accounts with a balance ≥ 10,000 USDT and a daily trading volume ≥ 30% of total funds, an extra 3% bonus yield applies, bringing the total APY to up to 10%. Compared with the industry average, APY offered by SunX remains significantly competitive.

SunX Online Q&A (Nov. 5, 2025)

**59\. If I don’t complete KYC on the** SunX **platform, how can I exchange USDT into fiat currency?**

As a decentralized perpetual futures trading platform, SunX does not provide fiat currency exchange services. You may transfer USDT to the HTX Exchange and then convert it to fiat through P2P trading.

**58\. What are the official Telegram (TG) accounts of** SunX **?**

The official SunX Telegram accounts are: @SunX\_Vivian, @mysticalwave, @sayonaraudin, @SunXbd, @ILoveyouEveryUniverss, @Nickky\_77, @Web3Donny, @PlusJhon, @jakolbhing, @Gdongdong, @nfree1125, @xiaoshuai\_945, @alyx\_SunX, @Jevon\_SunX, and @joy\_SunX. All of the above are officially verified community administrators or customer service representatives of SunX. We recommend contacting official public channels first. If private messaging is necessary, please verify the identity through these certified accounts to prevent impersonation scams.

**57\. I’ve added the wallet extension via Google Chrome, but it shows “wallet not detected". Do I need to log in first?**

Currently, SunX supports six major wallets: MetaMask, Binance Wallet, OKX Wallet, Bitget Wallet, TokenPocket, and TronLink. Please make sure your wallet was downloaded from official sources. Before connecting, ensure that you are logged in and the wallet is unlocked. If it still shows “wallet not detected", try restarting your browser or checking if the wallet extension is properly enabled.

**56\. When did SUN token buyback and burn start?**

The SUN token buyback and burn mechanism has been in continuous operation since March 2022, with a total of 648,535,242.90 $SUN burned to date. The most recent (48th) burn saw 2,060,843.918 $SUN destroyed, including: 362,655,328.09 $SUN repurchased and burned through SunSwap V2 revenue; 285,879,914.81 $SUN repurchased and burned through SunPump revenue. A detailed plan for allocating SunX platform revenue toward SUN token buyback and burn is currently being formulated. Please follow official announcements for updates.

# Order Type | SunX

Perpetual futures trading supports six order types: Limit Order, Market Order, Trigger Order, Post-Only, Trailing Order, and TWAP (Time-Weighted Average Price) Order.

1\. Limit Order

A limit order allows you to place a buy or sell order at a specified price or better. Execution is not guaranteed and only occurs if the market price reaches the preset price.

· Buy Limit Order: Executes at the preset price or lower.

· Sell Limit Order: Executes at the preset price or higher.

2\. Market Order

A market order is executed immediately at the best available market price.

· Only the futures contract type and amount are required; execution price depends on order book liquidity.

· Execution is guaranteed, but the order price cannot be specified.

3\. Trigger Order

A trigger order allows you to preset a trigger price, order price, and amount. Once the last traded price reaches the trigger price, the system automatically places the order with preset parameters.

· Supports both limit and market order types, following existing trading rules.

· Your assets will not be frozen until your trigger order is triggered.

· Trigger failure may come from price limits, insufficient balance, or system issues.

· Execution may fail even after your order is triggered due to market fluctuations.

o A limit order is placed at the preset price with execution subject to market conditions.

o A market order is executed at the current market price with execution subject to liquidity.

4\. Post-Only

A Post-Only order will not be executed immediately after being placed.

· Post-Only orders will be automatically canceled, if they match immediately with existing ones in the market.

· These orders ensure you always act as a maker (liquidity provider).

5\. Trailing stop

A trailing stop order allows you to set a stop price that follows the market as it moves in your favor. If the price reverses by a set percentage, it triggers a market order.

· Requires setting a trigger price and a callback rate. A limit order will be placed at the preset price after the conditions are reached.

· Use Cases: Buy on a rebound after a price drop; Sell on a pullback after a price rally.

6\. Time-Weighted Average Price (TWAP)

A TWAP order splits a large order into smaller portions over a set period, helping reduce market impact and improve execution price stability.

· Ideal for large orders, smooth entry/exit, or reducing timing risk.

· Parameters:

o Total Amount: Total contracts to buy or sell.

o Order Type: Limit order (preset price) or market order (best available market price).

o Order Splitting Rules:

§ By number of slices (e.g., 20)

§ By fixed single order size (e.g., 2 contracts per order)

o Interval: Time difference between two slices (e.g., 30 seconds, 1 minute).

o Validity Period: Total strategy duration or until all orders are filled.

# Mark Price | SunX

I. What is the Mark Price?

The contract mark price is a calculated, theoretical fair value price. It is not the real-time trading price you see on the exchange's order book.

Its core purpose is to accurately reflect the true market value of the underlying asset as much as possible, avoiding price abnormalities caused by insufficient liquidity or market manipulation on a single exchange.

Market Price: The actual price at which you open and close positions, determined by the latest trades on the exchange's order book. It is highly volatile.

Mark Price: The price used by the system to record your account's performance, calculating whether your position is profitable or loss-making and whether it will be liquidated. It is relatively smooth and fair.

II. How is the Mark Price Calculated?

The mark price is not arbitrarily set; it follows a universal calculation method, typically referencing two key factors:

(1) Spot Index Price

This serves as the foundation of the mark price. The system selects spot prices from several globally recognized, highly liquid, and trustworthy major exchanges.

(2) Funding Rate (Primarily for Perpetual Contracts)

Perpetual contracts have no expiration date. To ensure the contract price closely tracks the spot price, a "funding rate" mechanism is designed.

When market sentiment is bullish, long positions pay funding fees to short positions.

When market sentiment is bearish, short positions pay funding fees to long positions.

The calculation of the mark price incorporates the expectation of the funding rate, allowing it to predict the impact of funding rates on the contract price and thus more accurately anchor to the spot index price.

(3) Mark Price = Median (Funding Rate Basis Fair Price, Depth-Weighted Fair Price, EMA Latest Price)

If one of the three prices is excluded from the calculation (switch turned off), and the remaining two prices are denoted as a and b, then:

Mark Price = Median (Price a, Price b) = (Price a + Price b) / 2

If two of the three prices are excluded from the calculation (switch turned off), and the remaining price is denoted as x, then:

Mark Price = Price x

III. The Core Role of the Mark Price

The design of the mark price primarily serves risk control, with its key functions reflected in the following three aspects:

Preventing Malicious Liquidations

This is the most critical and important role of the mark price.

Problem: Without the mark price, the platform would use only the market price to calculate profits, losses, and liquidations. In a smaller exchange with poor liquidity, a large trader ("whale") could use a small amount of capital to suddenly crash or pump the market, causing extreme volatility in the market price and forcing the liquidation of大量 high-leverage users' positions. The price would then quickly return to normal, allowing the manipulator to profit. This behavior is known as "liquidation hunting" or "liquidation attack."

Solution: Using the mark price as the trigger standard for liquidations. Since the mark price is based on spot prices from multiple major exchanges, it is nearly impossible to manipulate by a single entity. It is extremely difficult for a manipulator to simultaneously manipulate spot prices across all major exchanges. This greatly protects ordinary traders and ensures the fairness of liquidations.

Fair Calculation of Unrealized Profit and Loss

Whether your position is profitable or loss-making should not fluctuate drastically due to temporary price abnormalities on a single exchange. The mark price provides a stable and fair benchmark for calculating your floating profits and losses.

Your unrealized P&L = (Mark Price - Your Average Entry Price) \* Contract Quantity

This calculation better reflects the true market value of your position rather than short-term market noise.

Serving as the Benchmark for Triggering Liquidations

Your margin ratio and liquidation price are calculated based on the mark price, not the market price.

Liquidation is only triggered when the mark price reaches your liquidation line.

This means that even if the market price on your exchange suddenly plummets, as long as the spot prices on global major exchanges (i.e., the mark price) have not fallen to your liquidation line, your position will not be liquidated.

# Forced Liquidation and Prices | SunX

I. Price Types

1\. Last Price

The last traded price of a futures contract, used in the calculation of realized PnL.

2\. Mark Price

A reference price calculated from the index price (based on a weighted average from multiple spot exchanges) and the funding rate. It is used to calculate unrealized PnL and to trigger liquidations.

a. Risk levels and maintenance margin ratios are dynamically changed based on the liquidation factor. Larger positions require a higher margin and have lower available leverage.

II. Forced Liquidation Trigger

Forced liquidation is triggered when the margin ratio ≥100% to prevent further losses.

Margin Formula:

· Initial margin = Face value per contract \* Position size / Average entry price / Leverage

· Maintenance margin = Average entry price \* Contract count \* Face value per contract / Leverage

How to Avoid Forced Liquidation:

When your risk ratio approaches 100%, you can reduce liquidation risk by adding margin to your account or reducing your position size.

III. Forced Liquidation Price

Forced liquidation occurs when the mark price reaches the liquidation threshold. Monitoring the gap between the mark price and the forced liquidation price is essential to avoid unexpected liquidation.

· In cross margin mode, long and short positions of the same contract share the same forced liquidation price.

IV. Forced Liquidation Process

1\. When your margin ratio is ≥100%, the system automatically triggers forced liquidation.

2\. All open (unfilled) orders in your account are immediately canceled.

3\. Depending on position size and risk ratio, the system may apply partial liquidation to reduce exposure before resorting to full liquidation.

V. Notes

· Position Size and Liquidation Type

o Smaller positions are more likely to be liquidated in full due to the limited margin buffer.

o Larger positions follow a tiered margin system, where liquidation is more gradual and risk control is more flexible.

· Suggestion

It is recommended to manually close positions before reaching the maintenance margin threshold, to avoid extra fees associated with forced liquidation.

· Negative Balance

If your account ends up with a negative balance after liquidation, you must deposit funds to restore the balance to positive.

[NextTrading Fees](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/trading-fees)

# Trading Fees | SunX

When you perform trades, SunX charges a fee (in USDT) on both opening and closing positions, which is factored into the realized profit and loss (PnL).

For example, in BTCUSDT perpetual futures trading, all fees are charged in USDT. These trading fees (or rebates for makers) are not frozen at the time of order placement; they are only deducted after execution and included in the realized PnL.

Formula: Trading fee = Number of executed contracts \* Face value per contract \* Execution price \* Trading fee rate

USDT-Margined Perpetual Futures Fee Rates:

Fee Rates to Open: Maker - 0.02%; Taker - 0.06%

Fee Rates to Close: Maker - 0.02%; Taker - 0.06%

Example 1: User A opens a long position of 200 conts (face value per cont: 0.001 BTC) in BTCUSDT perpetual futures at a price of 5,000 USDT, with the order filled as a taker. As the price rises after a few days, the user closes their position by placing a market order to sell all 200 conts at 6,000 USDT, with the order fully filled. Therefore:

Opening fee: 200 \* 0.001 \* 5,000 \* 0.06% = 0.6 USDT

Closing fee: 200 \* 0.001 \* 6,000 \* 0.02% = 0.24 USDT

Example 2: User B opens a long position of 200 conts (face value per cont: 0.01 ETH) in ETHUSDT perpetual futures at a price of 400 USDT, with the order filled as a taker. As the price rises after a few days, the user closes their position by placing a market order to sell all 200 conts at 480 USDT, with the order fully filled. Therefore:

Opening fee: 200 \* 0.001 \* 400 \* 0.06% = 0.48 USDT

Closing fee: 200 \* 0.001 \* 480 \* 0.02% = 0.192 USDT

Notes:

1\. The fee rates above are for illustration only. Please refer to your actual fee tier in the Fee Rates.

2\. Maker orders are limit orders added to the order book and pending execution, providing liquidity.

3\. When another user's open order executes against your pending order, you'll pay a maker fee.

4\. Taker orders are the limit or market orders that match immediately with existing orders in the book.

5\. When your pending order matches another user's open order, you need to pay a taker fee.

6\. A negative fee rate means you are not charged a fee; instead, you receive a rebate on the trade.

[NextTrading Account and Margin](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/trading-account-and-margin)

# Trading Account and Margin | SunX

1\. Margin Mode and Trading Account

Cross Margin: SunX currently supports the cross margin mode, which means all positions within your account share the same margin balance.

Isolated Margin: SunX temporarily does not support the isolated margin mode.

2\. Liquidation

For details on the liquidation process, please refer to the Liquidation section.

3\. Margin

In the futures market, you do not need to pay the full notional value of a trade. Instead, you just need to deposit a margin, a fraction of the contract value, as collateral to open and maintain positions. After a position is opened, the required margin is subject to change based on the last traded price.

Cross Margin Mode

SunX supports USDT as the primary margin asset. In cross margin mode, all positions under the same account, whether perpetual or delivery futures contracts, share the same account equity (i.e., USDT assets). Profits, losses, used margin, and margin ratio are calculated collectively.

Example: If User B holds a BTCUSDT perpetual position, an ETHUSDT perpetual position, and a BTCUSDT weekly delivery position in the cross margin mode, the USDT balance in the user's account backs all three positions, whose margin ratio will be calculated jointly. If the margin ratio exceeds 100%, the user faces potential liquidation on all three of their positions.

Note: Currently, SunX does not support the isolated margin mode. Please stay tuned for updates.

Margin Formula:

Position margin = Position value / Leverage

Example 1: Buy long 500 USDT worth of the BTCUSDT contract at a last price of 5,000 USDT per BTC, with 10x leverage. Position margin = 500 / 10 = 50 USDT

Example 2: Buy long 500 USDT worth of the ETHUSDT contract at a last price of 500 USDT per ETH, with 10x leverage. Position margin = 500 / 10 = 50 USDT

4\. Margin Optimization for Hedged Positions

To improve capital efficiency and reduce margin requirements, SunX applies a margin offset mechanism when users hold hedged (long and short) positions of the same contract under the same margin mode.

New position margin = Long position margin + Short position margin - Locked margin \* Locked margin offset

Position margin = Face value per contract \* Position size \* Last price / Leverage

Locked margin = min (Long position margin, Short position margin)

Note: In the cross margin mode, the new position margin equals the sum of the new position margins across all supported contracts.

[PreviousTrading Fees](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/trading-fees)
[NextLiquidation](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/liquidation)
