# Risk Reminder | SunX

1\. Liquidity Risk

The risk of being unable to open or close positions smoothly.

· Affected Parties: Traders and market makers

2\. Funding Rate Risk

The risk of potential losses caused by changes in funding fee direction or rising funding rates.

· Affected Parties: Traders and market makers

3\. Market Risk

The risk of potential losses due to price fluctuations of the underlying asset.

· Affected Parties: Traders, market makers, liquidity providers.

4\. Smart Contract Risk

The risk of potential losses caused by vulnerabilities in smart contracts.

· Note: While SunX has undergone rigorous testing and auditing, it is still in the testing phase. Undiscovered vulnerabilities may exist and could be exploited. Core smart contracts are non-upgradable, and users bear all risks associated with usage.

5\. Market Maker Risk

The risk of potential losses due to protocol malfunction caused by inactive or malicious behavior from market makers.

· Risk Management: Market makers are strictly vetted and required to stake assets. Malicious or non-compliant behavior may result in significant slashing of the staked cryptos.

· Affected Parties: Traders, market makers, liquidity providers.

6\. Slippage Risk

The risk of potential losses from price fluctuations between order submission and execution.

· Note: All trades are executed at the oracle price, eliminating market impact. Traders bear the risk of price fluctuations during the confirmation window.

7\. Liquidity Provider Risk

Liquidity providers (LPs) may be unable to withdraw funds when pool utilization is high.

· Affected Party: Liquidity providers

8\. Network Stability Risk

The risk of potential losses caused by network outages or congestion, which may prevent position opening/closing, liquidation, or minting/burning of liquidity tokens.

· Affected Parties: Traders, market makers, liquidity providers.

[PreviousOrder Type](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/order-type)
[NextForced Liquidation and Prices](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/forced-liquidation-and-prices)

Last updated 1 month ago

---

# Take-Profit and Stop-Loss | SunX

A Take Profit (TP) or Stop Loss (SL) order is a preset order to close positions with a trigger (TP price or SL price) and a specified order price. When the latest traded price reaches the preset trigger price, the system will automatically place the order to lock in profits or stop losses. Currently, there are two ways to place TP/SL orders:

New position: You can place a TP order and/or an SL order in advance when placing a limit order to open a position. Once the limit order is executed (either partially or fully), the system will automatically place the TP and/or SL order(s) based on your preset trigger and order prices.

Existing position: You can set a TP order and/or an SL order for an existing position. When the latest traded price reaches the trigger price, the system will automatically place the limit order at the predefined price and amount.

[PreviousLiquidation](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/liquidation)
[NextFunding Rate](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/funding-rate)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Liquidation | SunX

1\. Account Margin Ratio

Margin ratio = (Position size \* Average entry price \* Maintenance margin rate) / Net position value

Net position value = Margin + Unrealized PnL + Funding fee - Taker fee

2\. Maintenance Margin

Maintenance margin (MM) is the minimum amount of margin balance required to keep your positions open.

Formula:

Maintenance margin = Position size (crypto) \* Average entry price \* Maintenance margin rate

3\. Liquidation Trigger

Forced liquidation is automatically triggered when your account margin ratio is lower than or equal to the maintenance margin ratio (i.e., when the margin ratio rises to 100% or above).

· The liquidation process is executed within a single block to avoid price slippage risks.

4\. Post-Liquidation Handling

After liquidation, any remaining margin will be transferred into the Insurance Fund.

The insurance fund is used to offset platform losses when, under extreme market conditions, liquidation losses exceed the user's initial margin (i.e. "forced liquidation" or "negative equity").

5\. Notes

· Forced Liquidation/Negative Equity

They refer to situations where extreme volatility causes position losses greater than your initial margin.

· Insurance Fund

Acting as a risk control mechanism, it is designed to cover users' negative equity, ensuring system stability and overall security.

[PreviousTrading Account and Margin](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/trading-account-and-margin)
[NextTake-Profit and Stop-Loss](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/take-profit-and-stop-loss)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Funding Rate | SunX

I. Overview

Funding fees are a mechanism designed to ensure that the price of perpetual futures contracts aligns closely with their underlying asset's spot market price. These fees are periodically exchanged between traders holding long and short positions to incentivize the convergence of the futures price with the spot price.

· Funding fees are exchanged every hour between holders of long and short positions. The funding rate, which dictates the fee exchange, fluctuates in real-time.

· Only traders holding positions at the time of settlement are liable to either pay or receive funding fees.

· The calculation of the funding fees is based on the position value at the time of settlement, using the formula:

Funding fee = Position size \* Index price \* Funding rate

· Funding intervals (1h, 2h, 4h, 8h) vary by trading pair.

II. How Funding Rate Is Calculated

The funding rate consists of two parts: Interest Rate (I) and Average Premium Index (P).

Funding rate (F) = Average premium index (P) + Clamp (Interest (I) - Average premium index (P), 0.05%, -0.05%)

Hence, if (I - P) is within the range of ±0.05%, then F = P + (I - P) = I. In other words, the funding rate will equal the interest rate.

1\. Interest (I)

Formula

Interest (I) = (Quote currency interest rate - Base currency interest rate) / Funding frequency

· Quote currency interest rate: The interest rate for borrowing the quote currency

· Base currency interest rate: The interest rate for borrowing the base currency

· Funding frequency = 24 / Funding interval (hour)

2\. Average Premium Index (P)

Formula

Premium index (P) = \[Max (0, Impact bid price - Index price) - Max (0, Index price - Impact ask price)\] / Index price

· Impact bid price: The average fill price to execute the Impact Margin Notional on the Bid side.

· Impact Ask Price: The average fill price to execute the Impact Margin Notional on the Ask side.

· Impact margin notional (IMN) is the notion available to trade with a certain amount of margin. It's used to determine how deep the order book is and to measure the impact bid or ask price.

SunX calculates the average premium index (P) every minute by performing an N-hour Time-Weighted-Average-Price (TWAP) over the series of minute rates. (N = Funding interval) The closer to the funding fee settlement time, the greater the weight of the premium index.

Taking a 4-hour funding interval as an example, the average premium index (P) is calculated using the formula:

(Premium index a \* 2 + Premium index b \* 2 +... + Premium index n \* 240) / (1 + 2 +... + 240).

III. Summary

SunX calculates the premium index (P) and the interest rate (I) every minute, and then performs an N-hour Time-Weighted-Average-Price (TWAP) over the series of minute rates. Funding rates (F) adopt a damping mechanism of ±0.05% based on the average value to mitigate fluctuations.

Funding rates (F) are applied to a trader's position value to determine the funding fee to be paid or received at the funding timestamp.

[PreviousTake-Profit and Stop-Loss](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/take-profit-and-stop-loss)
[NextLast Price and Index Price](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/last-price-and-index-price)

# Last Price and Index Price | SunX

I. Last Price

Last Price refers to the last traded price of a futures contract, updated in real time and displayed in the order book. This metric, a must-watch especially for intraday traders and scalpers, reflects an immediate snapshot of current market conditions. It helps traders make timely decisions based on the latest data.

Primary Uses:

l Tracking the current market quotation.

l Calculating realized PnL (profit and loss from closed positions).

II. Index Price

Index Price is a fair price calculated with the weighted average of prices collected from multiple major crypto exchanges. These weights are dynamically updated every four hours to align with fluctuations on these platforms. Utilizing the index price helps you sidestep exchange-specific anomalies, making it advantageous for swing trading positions. Notably, this aggregated price is primarily used to calculate funding fees, ensuring fair funding rates across the market.

Primary Uses:

l Calculating unrealized PnL (i.e. floating profit and loss from open positions).

l Acting as the trigger benchmark for liquidations. A position is only liquidated if the index price reaches the liquidation threshold, helping prevent forced liquidations caused by malicious price manipulation on a single exchange.

III. Mark Price

Mark Price is a theoretical fair value calculated through a specific algorithm. Unlike the last price, it does not represent an actual trade on an exchange. It mainly reflects the true market value of an underlying asset and reduces the risk of unfair liquidations caused by thin liquidity or market manipulation.

· Market Price: The actual price at which orders are executed and closed on an exchange's order book, which can be highly volatile.

· Mark Price: A reference price used to calculate unrealized PnL and determine liquidation triggers. It is smoother, more stable, and fairer.

1\. How Mark Price is Calculated

The mark price is determined by the two key elements:

(1) Index price

Derived from aggregated spot prices across multiple major, highly liquid, and reliable global exchanges.

(2) Funding rate (for perpetual futures)

Ensures perpetual futures contracts track spot prices closely.

a. When the market is bullish, longs pay funding fees to shorts.

b. When the market is bearish, shorts pay funding fees to longs.

The expected funding rate adjustment is factored into the mark price calculation.

(3) Calculation method

The mark price is the median of the following three prices:

a. Funding basis fair price

b. Impact bid/ask price

c. Last EMA price

Special cases:

a. If one reference price is disabled, the mark price equals to the average of the remaining two, i.e., (a+b) / 2.

b. If two prices are disabled, the mark price equals to the remaining reference price.

2\. Mark Price's Core Functions

Mark Price is crucial for risk control and serves three main functions:

(1) Preventing unfair liquidations

Relying only on the market price for liquidations is risky because it's vulnerable to pumping and dumping by whales, which could push the price up and down in a short time to trigger a cascade of liquidations. That's why we use the mark price, a composite price across multiple spot markets, which smooths out these manipulation attempts and creates a fairer trading field for average traders.

(2) Fair calculation of unrealized PnL

Floating PnL is calculated based on the mark price to avoid extreme swings caused by temporary price anomalies on an exchange. Formula:

Unrealized PnL = (Mark price - Average entry price) \* Position size

This better reflects the true market value of open positions while filtering out short-term noise.

(3) Liquidation trigger benchmark

The system uses the mark price to calculate margin ratios and liquidation prices. A forced liquidation occurs only when the mark price reaches the liquidation price. This means traders are protected from being liquidated by temporary volatility in the local market.

[PreviousFunding Rate](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/funding-rate)
[NextTrading Rules](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/trade/trading-rules)

# Staking Rules | SunX

1.  How Can I Earn Rewards
    

Staking calculates rewards based on snapshots of the USDT assets in your SunX account. You only need to maintain USDT in your account to Staking rewards.

This feature does not affect your regular trading or deposit/withdrawal operations, and you can transfer assets in or out at any time.

1.  How can I earn staking rewards and what cryptos are included in the rewards?
    

You can earn rewards by holding/increasing the net equity of your USDT assets on SunX. The staking rewards currently consist of a 7% base APY (given in USDT) and a 3% APY boost (in TRX). You can claim your rewards at any time.

1.  How to Check Rewards Records
    

To view your daily rewards history, navigate to the "Unclaimed Rewards" section on the Staking page and click "Details".

1.  Reward Distribution
    

Once you manually claim your rewards, all participating crypto will be converted to USDT and deposited into your SunX account.

1.  Supported Cryptocurrencies
    

Staking only supports USDT assets. For a complete list of supported cryptocurrencies, please visit the Staking homepage.

1.  Interest-Bearing Principal Limits
    

Currently, there is no upper limit on the interest-bearing principal of USDT.

1.  How are staking rewards calculated?
    

Here's how staking rewards for Day T are calculated: On Day T+1, the rewards you earn on Day T will be calculated based on the snapshot of your asset balance, randomly taken from the previous 24 hours. Your rewards will be distributed after 17:00 on Day T+2 (UTC+8). (No staking rewards for the day of deposits). Example: User A stakes 10,000 USDT on Jan 1. Snapshots of their assets will be randomly taken on Jan 2, and rewards will be calculated on Jan 3. Rewards will be distributed starting at 17:00 (UTC+8) on Jan 4.

1.  How to earn an extra 3% APY?
    

If your snapshotted deposit balance is ≥10,000 USDT and you achieve a futures trading volume of ≥30% of your USDT balance on a day, you will earn an additional 3% APY on that day. Currently, the reward is distributed in TRX tokens and credited within 15 working days. We will support automatic reward distribution soon.

The interest-bearing principal limit is not fixed and may be adjusted dynamically by the platform without further notice.

The SunX platform will adjust the APY for its staking product to 10%, effective November 3, 2025 (UTC). This APY consists of two components, detailed below:

1\. 7% Base APY: Available to all users holding USDT with no minimum requirement. Staking rewards will be automatically paid in USDT.

l Maintain a snapshotted deposit balance of ≥10,000 USDT;

l Reach a futures trading volume of ≥30% of your USDT balance.

Currently, staking rewards for the Bonus APY will be paid in TRX tokens. Initial distributions will be handled manually within 15 working days, with automatic reward distribution coming soon.

The APY adjustment will become effective on November 3, 2025. Staking rewards accrued before this date will remain unchanged. Please stay tuned for future announcements regarding further updates.

# Invite Friends to Earn SunX Points and Redeem Them for USDT or an iPhone 17! | SunX

Dear SunX Users,

**Earn rewards by inviting friends!**

Invite friends to join SunX , earn SunX Points, and redeem them for **USDT, an iPhone 17**, and other premium rewards. It's easier to win an iPhone 17 with the SunX referral reward than to buy it yourself.

Event Period: 10:00 (UTC) on Oct 31 - 15:59 (UTC) on Nov 6

**How to Participate:**

1\. Copy Your Invitation Link: Log in to SunX and navigate to the [Referral](https://www.sunwukong.io/zh-cn/futures/invite/)
 page to copy your invitation link.

2\. Invite Friends: When your friends sign up via your link and complete the required tasks, both of you will earn points.

3\. Submit Your Invitation Code: Enter your SunX invitation code in the form to start accumulating points ([Click here to submit)](https://forms.gle/S2YJxKatAm6XdKxNA)

4\. Points Update: Invitation points will be updated daily before 13:00 (UTC) via Google Sheets.

**Reward Rules for Invitation Points:**

Earn points when your invitees complete tasks such as sign-ups, deposits, trading, or holding. Each user can earn up to 3,000 points.

[\>>Click here to submit your invitation code](https://forms.gle/S2YJxKatAm6XdKxNA)

**Points Redemption Rules:**

**Terms and Conditions:**

● SunX reserves the right for final interpretation of this event.

● Points for the asset-holding task are calculated based on the holding duration. Once the requirement is met, points will be automatically granted.

● Only invitees who connect their wallet for the first time during the event are eligible. The user who had already deposited or traded before binding a referral code isn't eligible for the event.

● The rewards will be credited to the winners' SunX accounts within 14 working days after the end of the event.

● Users who engage in self-trading, wash trading, mass mutual referrals using the same funds, or scripted instant trades are not eligible to claim rewards.

● Users found engaging in malicious volume manipulation or internal wash trades will be disqualified from the rewards.

● SunX reserves the right for final interpretation of this event.

# Refer Friends to Boost Your Earnings: Get 10% Fee Rebate + 10% Bonus! | SunX

Dear SunX Users,

Refer and Earn! High fee rebates and boosted bonuses are waiting for you. Simply invite friends to sign up and trade on SunX, and both you and your friends will receive generous rewards, making earning easier than ever.

Event Period: 16:00 (UTC) on Nov 10 - 15:59 (UTC) on Nov 18

**How to Participate?**

**● Copy Your Invitation Link:** Log in to SunX and navigate to the Referral page to copy your invitation link.

**● Invite Friends:** Use your invitation link to invite friends to sign up on SunX and complete the trading task.

**● Enjoy Rewards:** Both you and your invitee will receive fee rebates and additional bonuses based on actual trading volume.

[\>>Click here to submit your invitation code](https://forms.gle/iGhDCLoz1UZtoMC37)

**Reward Rules:**

Invite friends to SunX during this event. When your invitee signs up and reaches 200 USDT in trading volume, you'll both receive rewards! Details are provided below:

**● Invite 1 or more friends:**

○ Earn 5% fee rebate on your own trades.

○ Earn 20% bonus (original 15% + 5% boost) from your invitee's trades.

**● Invite 3 or more friends:**

○ Earn 10% fee rebate on your own trades.

○ Earn 25% bonus (original 15% + 10% boost) from your invitee's trades.

● Your invitee earns 5% fee rebate.

**Terms and Conditions:**

● The fee rebate is calculated from your own trading fees, while the bonus boost is calculated based on your invitee's trading fees.

● Only invitees who connect their wallet for the first time during the event are eligible. The user who had already deposited or traded before binding a referral code isn't eligible for the event.

● The rewards will be credited to the winners' SunX accounts within 14 working days after the end of the event.

● Users who engage in self-trading, wash trading, mass mutual referrals using the same funds, or scripted instant trades are not eligible to claim rewards.

● Users found engaging in malicious volume manipulation or internal wash trades will be disqualified from the rewards.

● SunX reserves the right for final interpretation of this event.

Thank you for your support and trust. We anticipate your participation!

SunX Team

# SunX Launches Airdrop Giveaway #1 - $5,000,000 for Arbitrum Community | SunX

To celebrate our rebranding, SunX is specially launching a series of Airdrop Giveaways. The inaugural phase offers $5,000,000 and is dedicated to rewarding users in the Arbitrum ecosystem. Generous rewards await you! Claim up to a $50,000 reward.

**I. Event Schedule**

• Event Start Time: 12:00 (UTC) on Nov 20, 2025

• Airdrop Query Deadline: 16:00 (UTC) on Jan 19, 2026

• Duration: 60 days

**II. Airdrop Eligibility Check**

• Eligibility: This airdrop is exclusively for Arbitrum wallet addresses.

• How to Check Eligibility: Please visit our official event page and enter your wallet address to check your eligibility.

**III. How to Claim Rewards**

Eligible users can claim airdrop rewards in just two simple steps:

**Step 1: Claim a Basic Reward**

1\. Connect your Arbitrum wallet address on the event page.

2\. Complete a trade of any pair worth at least 100 USDT on SunX.

3\. Claim an airdrop of $2-$300 on the event page.

**Step 2: Claim an Advanced Reward**

1\. Keep trading on SunX.

2\. Your Advanced Reward amount will be calculated based on your cumulative trading volume during the event.

3\. The Advanced Reward tiers vary; the more you trade, the larger the reward, with a maximum reward of $50,000.

**IV. Notes**

1\. Event rewards will be distributed in the form of USDT.

2\. Rewards can be claimed upon completion of the specified tasks.

3\. Rewards cannot be claimed after the event ends, so please claim your rewards promptly according to the event schedule.

4\. SunX will strictly monitor any malicious behavior, such as volume manipulation, wash trading, and self-trading. If such behavior is detected, SunX will revoke their qualification for the event.

5\. SunX reserves the right for the final interpretation of this event.

For users who do not qualify for this airdrop, please stay tuned for the upcoming phase.

# Join SunX Futures Trial Bonus Early Bird Program: Invite Friends and Unlock Exclusive Privileges | SunX

SunX Futures Trial Bonus is coming soon!

We're introducing the Futures Trial Bonus Early Bird Program, inviting you to be among the first users to experience it. With the Futures Trial Bonus, you can explore futures trading without risking your own capital, amplify potential profits, and reduce liquidation pressure.

By inviting friends to join, both of you will receive multiple exclusive benefits, including Futures Trial Bonuses, a fee-free first futures trade, and additional fee rebates. _This allows you to place your first futures trade with zero capital required._

Event Period: 10:00 (UTC) on Nov 17, 2025 - 15:59 (UTC) on Nov 20, 2025

[Register Now](https://forms.gle/sC8mBz9MxA7FMnok6)

Futures Trial Bonus: Can be used to offset a portion of futures trading fees, funding rates, or position losses. Detailed usage rules will be provided on the event page soon.

**Reward 1: Invite 1 Friend to Unlock the “Early Bird Officer” Status**

Invite one friend to sign up and complete a futures trade of ≥20 USDT on SunX . Once successful, both you and your invitee will receive the following rewards:

● For You (Inviter): 10 USDT Futures Trial Bonus + Early Bird Officer status.

● For Your Invitee: 5 USDT Futures Trial Bonus + a fee-free first futures trade, giving them a zero-cost start to futures trading.

**Reward 2: Invite More Friends to Unlock the “Supreme Experience Officer” Status**

The more friends you invite, the higher your rank and the greater your rewards. Earn increased Futures Trial Bonuses and gain the chance to access new platform features ahead of others.

**Officer Level**

**Invitees Needed**

**Rewards**

**Reward 3: Earn an Extra 10% Bonus to Boost Passive Income**

For invitees who sign up during the event, you’ll earn an additional 10% bonus on top of the base rate from the futures trading fees generated by your invitees within 7 days of their registration.

**Example:**

● Your invitee generates 100 USDT in futures trading fees.

● Your Earnings = 20 USDT (20% Base) + 10 USDT (10% Event Bonus)

● Total Bonus: 30 USDT

**Reward 4: Invitee's 7-Day Growth Gift — Unlock Futures Trial Bonuses and Fee Discounts**

If your invitee achieves a daily futures trading volume of ≥ 200 USDT, they can unlock up to 25 USDT in Futures Trial Bonuses plus a 10% fee discount:

● Trade ≥ 2 Days: Receive a 5 USDT Futures Trial Bonus.

● Trade ≥ 3 Days: Receive an 8 USDT Futures Trial Bonus.

● Trade ≥ 7 Days: Receive a 12 USDT Futures Trial Bonus + a 10% Trading Fee Discount (valid for 30 days).

**Terms and Conditions**

● Users must click “Register Now” to participate in the event and provide the correct referral code.

● The prize pool is set at 50,000 USDT in Futures Trial Bonuses and will be distributed in descending order according to the invitees' trading volumes.

● Only invitees who connect their wallet for the first time during the event are eligible. The user who had already deposited or traded before binding a referral code isn't eligible for the event.

● The rewards will be credited to the winners' SunX accounts within 14 working days after the end of the event.

● Users who engage in self-trading, wash trading, mass mutual referrals using the same funds, or scripted instant trades are not eligible to claim rewards.

● Users found engaging in malicious volume manipulation or internal wash trades will be disqualified from the rewards.

● SunX reserves the right for final interpretation of this event.

Thank you for your support and trust. We anticipate your participation!

SunX Team

# Rewards Worth $1.35 Million Are Here｜SunX's Trade to Earn #1 Is Live | SunX

Dear SunX Users,

In appreciation of your great support, SunX is excited to officially launch the Trade to Earn (Phase I) event. Simply make perpetual futures trades in our designated pairs, and you will get all your trading fees returned and win extra SUN tokens.

The event rewards will be distributed in $SUN. All net fees generated from registered participants trading the designated trading pairs during the event will be used for $SUN buybacks. This will provide you with an unprecedented opportunity for asset growth while ensuring stable $SUN appreciation.

[Trade Now>>](https://www.sunx.io/futures/tradeMining/)

**I. Event Period**

● Event Period: 12:00:00 (UTC) on November 21, 2025 – 12:00:00 (UTC) on December 6, 2025

● The "Trade & Earn" event is on a daily basis. A day is defined from 12:00 (UTC) on Day T to 12:00 (UTC) on Day T+1.

● The daily prize pool is divided into 24 portions, with a new portion released every hour.

● Event rewards will be calculated and updated starting on Day T+2 at 04:00 (UTC). Please claim your $SUN in time.

**II. Event Rules**

● Eligibility: Register to participate in the event.

● Applicable Trading Pairs: BTCUSDT, ETHUSDT, and SUNUSDT

● Prize Pools:

● Daily Prize Pool: 90,000 USDT in $SUN

● Total Prize Pool: 1,350,000 USDT in $SUN

● The daily prize pool is a fixed value in USDT, and the event will calculate the $SUN amount in each pool based on the $SUN price at the start of the day.

● For instance, if the $SUN price is 0.03 USDT at 12:00 (UTC) on Day T when the event starts, and the prize pool of the day is 90,000 USDT, then the total $SUN amount for the day would be 3,000,000 $SUN.

**III. Reward Calculation**

● Reward Formula: Reward Amount = User's Actual Trading Fees (USDT) for the Day × Corresponding Reward Percentage ÷ $SUN Price at 12:00 (UTC) on Day T.

● Reward Rate:

Maker: 110%

Taker: 107%

● Hourly Reward Cap for Each User: 500 USDT in $SUN.

For example, assume that the $SUN price is 0.03 USDT at the start of the "Trade to Earn" event at 12:00 (UTC) on Day T, and a participant generates 100 USDT in fees from BTC/USDT trading pair between 12:00 (UTC) on Day T and 11:59 (UTC) on Day T+1, all as Maker orders, and that the fees are generated before the depletion of the prize pool and the participant's reward cap is not reached,

the participant's daily reward of $SUN will be: 100 × 110% ÷ 0.03 = 3,667.

Rewards will be updated and made available for claim at 04:00 (UTC) on Day T+2.

**IV. $SUN Buyback and Burn Mechanism**

All net fees generated from registered participants trading the designated trading pairs during the event will be used for $SUN buybacks, ensuring stable appreciation of $SUN. $SUN token buyback will take place on the HTX platform, and the repurchased $SUN will be entirely burnt, with the schedule at the end of each quarter. Specific timing will be announced separately.

To facilitate buyback calculations, the daily trading fee statistics period is set from 00:00 to 23:59 (UTC+8) each day. The event starts at 20:00:00 (UTC+8) on T day. The first trading fee calculation period will be from 00:00 (UTC+8) to 23:59 (UTC+8) on T+1 day. The first buyback, based on trading fees generated on T+1 day, will be completed on T+2 day.

For the details of daily buyback after the event starts, please refer to further announcements.

[$SUN Buyback Details for "Trade to Earn" Event](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/activity/usdsun-buyback-details-for-trade-to-earn-event)

**V. Notes**

● $SUN will be distributed on the SunX platform. Users are recommended to participate via the Tron blockchain network. If other blockchains are chosen, SunX plans to launch a one-click $SUN-to-USDT exchange feature in Q4 2025. Stay tuned!

● Market makers are not eligible to participate in this event.

● During the event, there is a cap on the rewards that each participant can receive per hour. Participants will not be able to receive additional rewards if they reach their individual reward limit or if the overall prize pool limit is reached.

● Participants in the "Trade to Earn" event will receive a portion of their trading fees as a reward. No referral bonuses will be paid to the referrer until the prize pool is depleted, but all other trading-fee-based referral bonuses remain unaffected.

● Trading rewards will be distributed after deducting rewards from the Welcome Hub- Daily Trading Contest.

● SunX reserves the right to disqualify users engaging in cheating and revoke their rewards.

● SunX reserves the right for final interpretation of this event.

Thank you for your support and trust. We eagerly anticipate your participation!

SunX Team

Dear Users,

The SunPerp has been officially rebranded to SunX! Invite like-minded trading partners to share 1 Million $SUN growth bonuses, compounded with the Welcome Fiesta rewards and 20% referral bonus — all in together for the next chapter of professional trading.

**Event Period:** 10:00 (UTC) on Nov 24 - 09:59 (UTC) on Dec 3

[Invite now>>](https://forms.gle/htnDfdxg4K7z1bnv6)

**How to Participate in the Referral Program?**

1\. Get your referral link: Log into SunX, and navigate to the [Referral page](https://www.sunx.io/futures/invite/)
 to get your exclusive referral link or code.

2\. Share with friends: Send your referral link or code to your friends. They connect their wallet via the link or input your code under the Link Referral Relationship.

3\. Earn rewards: When your friends complete the trading tasks, both of you could receive rewards.

[Click here to view more>>](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/points-and-rewards/how-to-get-or-bind-the-referral-code)

**Event Details:**

For each successful referral you earn up to 130 $SUN, and your friend earns up to 130 $SUN. A total of 1 million $SUN is ready to be shared by you and your friends!

● First Trade Bonus

If your invitee completes their first trade of ≥300 USDT, you’ll receive 30 $SUN, and they’ll get 20 $SUN.

● 7-Day Milestone Bonus

If your invitee reaches a trading volume of ≥20,000 USDT within 7 days, you’ll both earn 100 $SUN.

\*You can enjoy rewards from this event together with the Welcome Fiesta rewards and the 20% referral bonus.

**Terms and Conditions**

● The total prize pool is 1 million $SUN. If the number of winners exceeds the pool limit, rewards will be distributed based on invitees’ trading volumes in descending order until the pool is exhausted.

● Only invitees who connect their wallet for the first time during the event are eligible. The user who had already deposited or traded before binding a referral code isn't eligible for the event.

● Within 3 days after the event ends, both the inviter and the invitee will be eligible for rewards if the invitee’s net deposit is ≥ 10 USDT.

● The rewards are accumulative and will be credited to the winners' SunX accounts within 14 working days after the end of the event.

● Users who engage in self-trading, wash trading, mass mutual referrals using the same funds, or scripted instant trades are not eligible to claim rewards.

● Users found engaging in malicious volume manipulation or internal wash trades will be disqualified from the rewards.

● SunX reserves the right for final interpretation of this event.

Thank you for your support and trust. We anticipate your participation!

Dear SunX Users,

In appreciation of your great support, SunX is thrilled to officially launch phase 2 of the Trade to Earn event. Simply make perpetual futures trades in our designated pairs, and you will get all your trading fees returned and win extra SUN tokens.

The event rewards will be distributed in $SUN. All trading fees generated from registered participants trading the designated trading pairs during the event will be used for $SUN buybacks. This will provide you with an unprecedented opportunity for asset growth while ensuring stable $SUN appreciation.

[**Register Now>>**](https://www.sunx.io/futures/tradeMining/)

**I. Event Schedule**

● Event Period: 12:00:00 (UTC) on Dec 10, 2025 - 12:00:00 (UTC) on Dec 25, 2025

● The Trade to Earn event is on a daily basis. A day is defined from 12:00 (UTC) on Day T to 12:00 (UTC) on Day T+1.

● The daily prize pool is divided into 24 portions, with each portion released on the hour.

● Rewards are calculated and updated hourly. You can claim your $SUN rewards from the second hour after each session ends.

**II. Event Rules**

● Eligibility: Anyone who registers for the event.

● Applicable Trading Pairs: BTCUSDT, ETHUSDT, and SUNUSDT

**○** For instance, if the $SUN price is 0.02 USDT at 12:00 (UTC) on Day T when the event starts, and the prize pool of the hour (12:00 - 13:00) for BTCUSDT is 1,458 USDT, i.e., 72,900 $SUN (= 1,458 / 0.02).

# 14 Days Only: Share a Million-Dollar Airdrop for SunX Trial Bonus Launch | SunX

Dear SunX Users,

SunX is thrilled to announce the official launch of our new "Trial Bonus" feature and is celebrating with a 14-day airdrop event! Both new and existing users are invited to share a total prize pool of million-dollar trial bonuses.

**Event Period:** 16:00 (UTC) on Dec 12, 2025 - 15:59 (UTC) on Dec 26, 2025

**How to Get an Airdrop?**

Meet any one of the following three requirements to claim a 5 USDT Futures Trial Bonus.

1\. For Existing Traders: Reach a cumulative futures trading volume of ≥1,000 USDT between September 19, 2025 and 15:59 (UTC) on December 12, 2025.

2\. For Active Traders: Reach a cumulative futures trading volume of 5,000 USDT during the event.

3\. For New Users: Complete your first futures trade of ≥1,000 USDT during the event period.

**How to Participate?**

Fill out the [**form**](https://forms.gle/uZXCDtzSnX9TFJUX7)
 to register for the event. The platform will automatically distribute an airdrop to every eligible user.

**Terms and Conditions:**

1\. The daily prize pool is set at 80,000 USDT in futures trial bonuses. The bonuses are distributed on a first-come, first-served basis according to the order in which conditions are met.

2\. Participants cannot win rewards from both this event and other promotions of the same kind.

3\. The USDT rewards are given in the form of trial bonuses. Rewards will be distributed to winners who do not claim their rewards every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday.

4\. Futures trial bonuses can be used to offset a portion of futures trading fees, funding fees, or position losses. Detailed usage rules are provided on the event page.

5\. The claim and usage validity period for a trial bonus is 3 days. Please claim and use it promptly.

6\. This event is not open to market makers. Participants involved in using bots, cheating, or duplicate registration will be disqualified. Using multiple accounts will also result in disqualification from rewards.

7\. Only trading volume with trading fees paid is counted towards this event. Trades with zero trading fees, negative maker fees, or trial bonuses are not included in the volume calculation for the event.

8\. SunX reserves the right for final interpretation of this event.

SunX Team

# Referral Program | SunX

**How It Works**

1\. Generate your invitation code on the Referral page and share it with your friends.

2\. Inviters can only customize their invitation code once.

3\. After the invitee completes signup, the information on the inviter's Referral page will be updated in real time.

4\. Both custom invitation codes and default invitation codes can be used unlimited times.

5\. Inviters earn a 15% referral bonus from their invitees' trading fees, while invitees enjoy a 5% discount on trading fees.

6\. Once the referral relationship is established, it cannot be changed, and there is no limit to the number of invitees.

7\. Referral bonus rates may be adjusted based on market conditions or platform policies. Users will be notified of any updates via announcements or direct notifications.

**Bonus Settlement and Tracking**

l Referral bonuses will be distributed in USDT to your account.

l Each trading fee generated by your invitee, except for those with negative fee rates, will earn you a corresponding referral bonus.

l Bonus amount (USDT) = Trading volume \* Trading fee rate \* Bonus rate.

l You can view your full bonus history on the Referral page.

l The referral bonus data is updated based on the UTC+8 time zone, and enters a maintenance period daily after 20:00. Data during maintenance per day is based on prior-day assets and may show slight discrepancies or delays.

**Terms**

l If an invitee violates any referral bonus risk management rule, their inviter will not receive the bonus. In addition, the invitee's referral status will be marked as \[Invalid\], and any generated bonus records will be marked as \[Invalid bonus\].

l Only new users who sign up using your referral link are eligible.

l Self-referrals (creating multiple accounts to invite yourself) are not allowed. If detected, all referral bonuses will be revoked.

l Offensive, misleading, or harmful custom invitation codes may result in removal from the program and cancellation of bonuses.

l The referrer acts independently and is responsible for understanding the risks and legal implications of promoting futures trading in their region.

l SunX may extend the validity period of referrals at its discretion.

l SunX reserves the right to modify bonus rates, program rules, or cancel the referral program at any time.

l SunX also reserves the right to interpret the terms of the program.

# How to get or bind the referral code? | SunX

**How to get the referral code?**

1\. Open the [Sunx website and go to the Referral page](https://www.sunperp.com/futures/invite/)
, then click “Connect Wallet”;

\*SunX currently supports Tronlink, Bitget Wallet, OKX Wallet, TokenPocket, and Binance Wallet.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252F9inxGmWOW81uxxWg6w7t%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15dcc0d9-3a46-42c7-a253-0484851975d2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8dafa365&sv=2)

**2\. Once a wallet is connected, a default referral code will be automatically generated.**

Users can upgrade their default referral code to a custom one consisting of 5–12 letters or a combination of letters and numbers. This helps improve shareability and strengthen personal branding. Once created, the custom code cannot be modified or deleted, so please set it carefully.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FkgW7tbRdaz0lvxUDESCX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d9e923d-0806-4b49-a8b1-b3460740bba8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e39a0226&sv=2)

**How to share the referral code?**

Share your referral link or code with friends through the following methods. When your friend accepts the invitation, both parties will share 20% commission.

The inviter will earn a 15% commission on fees from the invitee’s trades and the invitee will enjoy a 5% rebate on trading fees.

1\. After connecting your wallet, go to the Referral page to directly copy and share your referral code.

2\. Guide your friends to bind the referral code manually: Ask your friends to go to the [Referral page >> Bind Inviter](https://www.sunperp.com/futures/invite/)
, enter your code manually and complete the binding.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252Fi9l0V8EfGkGLK2OTiqxR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D104d115f-cb6d-44c2-a2ca-d23fb99da98f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=34e3a96b&sv=2)

**How to view referral relationships and commission?**

When your invited friend binds your referral code and completes a transaction on SunX, you will receive your commission before 12:00 (UTC) on the following day. All commission details can be viewed on the [Referral page](https://www.sunperp.com/zh-cn/futures/invite/)
.

\*Notes: During the daily maintenance period, displayed data is based on the previous day’s asset status, so slight discrepancies or temporary delays may occur.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252Fyq9K1pppCU0YL6g1xJ9e%252F3-%25E8%25BF%2594%25E4%25BD%25A3%25E6%2594%25B6%25E7%259B%258A-EN.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4e84230-9a91-4222-ac44-89ef98819975&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b423ed90&sv=2)

**How can invitees accept an invitation?**

Invitees can accept an invitation and enjoy a 5% rebate on trading fees through either of the following methods:

**1\. Bind a wallet via the referral link**

After opening the referral link, click “Connect Wallet”, select a wallet to connect, and complete the connection to enjoy a 5% rebate on trading fees.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252Fy6uDPmW53LSJPONNeqgt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D206da8d6-0b4a-45a7-96f3-ca0cb9593179&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c7f3b031&sv=2)

**2\. Bind a referral code on the Referral page**

If the wallet was not connected through the referral link, the user can go to the Referral page >> Bind Inviter and enter the referral code to establish the referral relationship.

![](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3599393801-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLJp5Dq9Iikvq07PruZg8%252Fuploads%252FIBeaHyaocIZNJuLTpL5Y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dae4d4fbe-74c8-4122-81df-f7e4851d5f74&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=95e01bef&sv=2)

**Notes:**

● The rules and details of the SunX Referral Reward Program may be adjusted as needed and SunX reserves the right to update the program terms in response to market changes.

● Any form of abuse such as self-invitation, offline rebates, or other improper use is strictly prohibited. SunX reserves the right to restrict or revise participation conditions in such cases.

# SunX Affiliate Referral Program | SunX

1\. SunX Commission Rate Tiers and Assessment Criteria

The SunX platform categorizes affiliate commissions into three tiers based on the percentage of commissions an inviter can earn, with higher tiers offering higher rates. To qualify for a specific tier, an inviter must meet any one of the "Inviter Requirements" and contact their business manager. See the table below for details:

Tier

Commission Rate

Inviter Requirements (Meeting Any of the Three Criteria)

Invitee Requirement

Level 1

30%

1\. Individual Trading Volume: 30-day weighted trading volume ≥$500,000

2\. Team Size: Cumulative referrals ≥10 invitees (with ≥5 active traders in a natural month)

3\. Trading Volume Scale: Natural month trading volume ≥$1,000,000

No specific requirement

Level 2

40%

1\. Individual Trading Volume: 30-day weighted trading volume ≥$2,500,000

2\. Team Size: Cumulative referrals ≥20 invitees (with ≥5 active traders in a natural month, including at least 1 reaching VIP2)

3\. Trading Volume Scale: Natural month trading volume ≥$5,000,000

Invitee must be VIP2 (30-day weighted trading volume ≥$1,000,000)

Level 3

50%

1\. Individual Trading Volume: 30-day weighted trading volume ≥$5,000,000

2\. Team Size: Cumulative referrals ≥50 invitees (with ≥10 active traders in a natural month, including at least 3 reaching VIP2 or 1 reaching VIP3)

3\. Trading Volume Scale: Natural month trading volume ≥$10,000,000

1\. Invitee must be VIP2 (30-day weighted trading volume ≥$1,000,000), or 2. Invitee must be VIP3 (30-day weighted trading volume ≥$5,000,000)

2\. Commission Rate Tiers Adjustment (Upgrade & Downgrade)

Assessment Cycle: SunX will evaluate all Affiliates monthly. The evaluation criteria will be based on the requirements necessary to reach each commission tier.

Upgrade: The monthly assessment begins at 00:00:00 (UTC+8) on the first day of each calendar month. The affiliate's cumulative data will be evaluated, and their commission tier will be updated within the first business week of the following month. If an Affiliate meets the criteria for a higher tier, they will be upgraded and receive the corresponding commission rate, capped at 50%.

Example: If you are a Level 2 Inviter (40% commission) in October and meet any Level 3 criteria during that month's assessment, you will be upgraded to Level 3 (50% commission) within the first business week in November.

Downgrade: The monthly assessment begins at 00:00:00 (UTC+8) on the first day of each calendar month. The affiliate's cumulative data will be evaluated, and their commission tier will be updated within the first business week of the following month. If an affiliate fails to meet the requirements of their current tier during the assessment, their level will be downgraded to the highest tier they still qualify for. After the downgrade, invitees' discount rates remain unchanged, while the affiliate's commission rate adjusts to the new tier.

Example: If you are a Level 2 Inviter (40% commission) in October but fail to meet any Level 2 criteria, you will be downgraded to Level 1 (30% commission) within the first business week in November.

3\. VIP Client Commission Retention Rate

Bonus Amount (USDT) = Trading Volume \* Trading Fee Rate \* Commission Rate \* Inviter Retention Rate

SunX VIP Tier

30D Weighted Trading Volume ($)

Inviter Retention Rate (Amount Kept)

1

≤1,000,000

100%

2

\>1,000,000

100%

3

\>5,000,000

90%

4

\>25,000,000

80%

5

\>100,000,000

70%

6

\>500,000,000

60%

4\. Resolving Commission Overlaps Between Affiliates and Brokers

If a user with an existing upline inviter places an order using a broker ID other than their inviter's, 30% of the commission will go to the broker, and the remaining 70% will still be paid to the user's upline inviter.

5\. Terms and Conditions:

l Commission settlement and distribution occur daily between 20:00–21:00 (UTC+8) on the T+1 day.

l All SunX referral relationships are permanently valid by default.

l There is no limit to the number of invitees you can refer.

l Only new users who register via your referral link are eligible.

l Self-referrals (creating multiple accounts to invite yourself) are prohibited. If detected, all referral bonuses will be revoked.

l SunX commission rules are subject to updates.

l SunX reserves the right to modify program rules or cancel the referral program at any time.

l SunX reserves the right for final interpretation of this program.

# Error code | SunX

Error Code

Error Description

500

System error

1010

The user does not exist.

1066

This field cannot be left empty.

1067

Invalid field

4010

Deduction is not yet enabled.

4012

The crypto is unavailable for deduction.

4014

Setting fee deduction is temporarily unavailable. Please contact your account manager for assistance.

6001

The Single-Asset Collateral mode is temporarily unavailable.

6002

The Multi-Assets Collateral mode is temporarily unavailable.

6003

Update your app to the latest version to use the Multi-Assets Collateral mode.

6004

Switching margin mode is unavailable due to ADL.

6005

Switching margin mode is unavailable due to liquidation.

6006

Switching margin mode is unavailable as trading is disabled.

6007

Switching...

6008

Failed to switch your collateral mode.

6009

Switching mode is unavailable due to negative equity.

6010

The current margin mode is as you required.

6011

Placing orders is unavailable due to ADL or liquidation.

6012

Your account is in liquidation or ADL. Please retry later.

6013

The position is in liquidation or ADL. Please retry later.

6014

Multi-Assets Collateral mode is currently unavailable. For any questions, please contact customer service.

6015

Opening positions under the Multi-Assets Collateral mode is currently unavailable. For any questions, please contact customer service.

6016

Closing positions under the Multi-Assets Collateral mode is currently unavailable. For any questions, please contact customer service.

14610

The size of a long position cannot exceed {0} {1}. Please retry.

14620

The size of a short position cannot exceed {0} {1}. Please retry.

4013

The current Futures Grid is being retired soon. To create new grids, please go to Trading Bots and experience our new Futures Grid.

50222

This service is unavailable for Fireblocks sub-accounts.

50224

Unavailable

50225

Please create a Fireblocks CVA address.

50226

The feature is temporarily unavailable for custodial sub-accounts.

# Media Kit | SunX

Please follow these guidelines when using SunX brand assets:

All SunX brand assets are copyrighted materials. Please get approval from SunX before using them.

Where possible, hyperlink our brand assets to SunX's official website and social media channels like X (Twitter).

Use our brand assets when announcing official partnerships.

Avoid the following:

Don't use SunX brand assets for promoting your own project, especially without our consent.

Don't repurpose any SunX brand elements (logos, visuals, colors, etc.).

Get in touch

For any questions about using SunX 's brand assets, or for partnerships, brokerage inquiries, influencer collaborations, or referral opportunities, please contact support@sunx.io.

# Preparation | SunX

Before you use API, you need to login the website to create API Key with proper permissions. The API key is shared for all instruments in SunX including spot, futures, swap, options.

You can manage your API Keys [here](https://www.sunperp.com/futures/api-manage/)
.

Every user can create at most 20 API Keys, each can be applied with either permission below:

*   Read permission: It is used to query the data, such as order query, trade query.
    
*   Trade permission: It is used to create order, cancel order and transfer, etc.
    
*   Withdraw permission: It is used to create withdraw order, cancel withdraw order, etc.
    

Please remember below information after creation:

*   `Access Key` It is used in API request
    
*   `Secret Key` It is used to generate the signature (only visible once after creation)
    

The API Key can bind maximum 20 IP addresses (either host IP or network IP), we strongly suggest you bind IP address for security purpose. The API Key without IP binding will be expired after 90 days.**Warning** : These two keys are important to your account safety, please don't share **both** of them together to anyone else . If you find your API Key is disposed, please remove it immediately.

[PreviousQuick start](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start)
[NextInterface Type](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/interface-type)

Last updated 1 month ago

---

# Interface Type | SunX

There are two types of interface, you can choose the proper one according to your scenario and preferences.

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/interface-type#rest-api)

REST API

REST (Representational State Transfer) is one of the most popular communication mechanism under HTTP, each URL represents a type of resource.

It is suggested to use Rest API for one-off operation, like trading and withdraw.

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/interface-type#websocket-api)

WebSocket API

WebSocket is a new protocol in HTML5. It is full-duplex between client and server. The connection can be established by a single handshake, and then server can push the notification to client actively.

It is suggest to use WebSocket API to get data update, like market data and order update.

**Authentication**

Both API has two levels of authentication:

Public API: It is for basic information and market data. It doesn't need authentication.

Private API: It is for account related operation like trading and account management. Each private API must be authenticated with API Key.

[PreviousPreparation](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/preparation)
[NextAuthentication](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/authentication)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Authentication | SunX

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/authentication#overview)

Overview

The API request may be tampered during internet, therefore all private API must be signed by your API Key (Secrete Key).

Each API Key has permission property, please check the API permission, and make sure your API key has proper permission.

A valid request consists of below parts:

*   API Path: for example api.sunx.io/sapi/v1/trade/order
    
*   API Access Key: The 'Access Key' in your API Key
    
*   Signature Method: The first one is for users to use the elliptic curve digital signature algorithm, using Ed25519. ‌The second, hash-based protocol for user-computed signatures, uses HmacSHA256.
    
*   Ed25519 introduction: It is a high-performance digital signature algorithm that provides fast signature verification and generation while having high security.
    
*   Signature Version: The version for the signature protocol, it uses **2**
    
*   Timestamp: The UTC time when the request is sent, e.g. 2017-05-11T16:22:06. It is useful to prevent the request to be intercepted by third-party.
    
*   Parameters: Each API Method has a group of parameters, you can refer to detailed document for each of them.
    
    *   For GET request, all the parameters must be signed.
        
    *   For POST request, the parameters needn't be signed and they should be put in request body.
        
    
*   Signature: The value after signed, it is guarantee the signature is valid and the request is not be tempered.
    

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/authentication#undefined)

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/authentication#ed25519-signature-method)

Ed25519 Signature Method

The signature may be different if the request text is different, therefore the request should be normalized before signing. Below signing steps take the order query as an example:

This is a full URL to query one order:

[https://api.sunx.io/sapi/v1/trade/order?](https://api.sunx.io/sapi/v1/trade/order?)

`AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx`

`&SignatureMethod=Ed25519`

`&SignatureVersion=2`

`&Timestamp=2017-05-11T15:19:30`

`&order_id=1234567890`

**1\. The request Method (GET or POST, WebSocket use GET), append line break "\\n"**

`GET\n`

**2\. The host with lower case, append line break "\\n"**

`Example:api.sunx.io\n`

**3\. The path, append line break "\\n"**

For example, query orders:

`/sapi/v1/trade/order\n`

`For example, WebSocket v1`

`/ws/v1`

**4\. The parameters are URL encoded, and ordered based on ASCII**

For example below is the original parameters:

`AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx`

`order_id=1234567890`

`SignatureMethod=Ed25519`

`SignatureVersion=2`

`Timestamp=2017-05-11T15%3A19%3A30`

Use UTF-8 encoding and URL encoded, the hex must be upper case. For example, The semicolon ':' should be encoded as '%3A', The space should be encoded as '%20'.The 'timestamp' should be formated as 'YYYY-MM-DDThh:mm:ss' and URL encoded. The value is valid within 5 minutes.

Then above parameter should be ordered like below:

`AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx`

`SignatureMethod=Ed25519`

`SignatureVersion=2`

`Timestamp=2017-05-11T15%3A19%3A30`

`order_id=1234567890`

**5\. Use char "&" to concatenate all parameters**

`AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx&SignatureMethod=Ed25519&SignatureVersion=2&Timestamp=2017-05-11T15%3A19%3A30&order_id=1234567890`

**6\. Assemble the pre-signed text**

`GET\n`

`api.sunx.io\n`

`/sapi/v1/trade/order\n`

`AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx&SignatureMethod=HmacSHA256&SignatureVersion=2&Timestamp=2017-05-11T15%3A19%3A30&order_id=1234567890`

**7\. Use the pre-signed text and your Secret Key to generate a signature**

*   Use the request string obtained in the previous step to generate the private key of Ed25519 and add it to generate a signature.
    
*   Encode the generated signature with base-64, and the resulting value is used as the digital signature of this interface call.
    

`4F65x5A2bLyMWVQj3Aqp+B4w+ivaA7n5Oi2SuYtCJ9o=`

**8\. Put the signature into request URL**

For Rest interface:

1.  Put all the parameters in the URL
    
2.  Encode signature by URL encoding and append in the URL with parameter name "Signature".
    

Finally, the request sent to API should be:

[https://api.sunx.io/sapi/v1/trade/order?AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx&order\_id=1234567890&SignatureMethod=Ed25519&SignatureVersion=2&Timestamp=2017-05-11T15%3A19%3A30&Signature=4F65x5A2bLyMWVQj3Aqp%2BB4w%2BivaA7n5Oi2SuYtCJ9o%3D](https://api.sunx.io/sapi/v1/trade/order?AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx&order_id=1234567890&SignatureMethod=Ed25519&SignatureVersion=2&Timestamp=2017-05-11T15%3A19%3A30&Signature=4F65x5A2bLyMWVQj3Aqp%2BB4w%2BivaA7n5Oi2SuYtCJ9o%3D)

For WebSocket interface:

1.  Fill the value according to required JSON schema
    
2.  The value in JSON doesn't require URL encode
    

For example:

Private channel subscription:

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/authentication#hmacsha256-signature-method)

`HmacSHA256` Signature Method

The signature may be different if the request text is different, therefore the request should be normalized before signing. Below signing steps take the order query as an example:

This is a full URL to query one order:

[https://api.sunx.io/sapi/v1/trade/order?](https://api.sunx.io/sapi/v1/trade/order?)

`AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx`

`&SignatureMethod=HmacSHA256`

`&SignatureVersion=2`

`&Timestamp=2017-05-11T15:19:30`

`&order_id=1234567890`

**1\. The request Method (GET or POST, WebSocket use GET), append line break "\\n"**

`GET\n`

**2\. The host with lower case, append line break "\\n"**

`Example:api.sunx.io\n`

**3\. The path, append line break "\\n"**

For example, query orders:

`/sapi/v1/trade/order\n`

`For example, WebSocket v2`

`/ws/v2`

**4\. The parameters are URL encoded, and ordered based on ASCII**

For example below is the original parameters:

`AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx`

`order_id=1234567890`

`SignatureMethod=HmacSHA256`

`SignatureVersion=2`

`Timestamp=2017-05-11T15%3A19%3A30`

Use UTF-8 encoding and URL encoded, the hex must be upper case. For example, The semicolon ':' should be encoded as '%3A', The space should be encoded as '%20'.The 'timestamp' should be formated as 'YYYY-MM-DDThh:mm:ss' and URL encoded. The value is valid within 5 minutes.

Then above parameter should be ordered like below:

`AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx`

`SignatureMethod=HmacSHA256`

`SignatureVersion=2`

`Timestamp=2017-05-11T15%3A19%3A30`

`order_id=1234567890`

**5\. Use char "&" to concatenate all parameters**

`AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx&SignatureMethod=HmacSHA256&SignatureVersion=2&Timestamp=2017-05-11T15%3A19%3A30&order_id=1234567890`

**6\. Assemble the pre-signed text**

`GET\n`

`api.sunx.io\n`

`/sapi/v1/trade/order\n`

`AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx&SignatureMethod=HmacSHA256&SignatureVersion=2&Timestamp=2017-05-11T15%3A19%3A30&order_id=1234567890`

**7\. Use the pre-signed text and your Secret Key to generate a signature**

*   Use the pre-signed text in step 6 and your API Secret Key to generate hash code by HmacSHA256 hash function.
    
*   Encode the hash code with base-64 to generate the signature.
    

`4F65x5A2bLyMWVQj3Aqp+B4w+ivaA7n5Oi2SuYtCJ9o=`

**8\. Put the signature into request URL**

For Rest interface:

1.  Put all the parameters in the URL
    
2.  Encode signature by URL encoding and append in the URL with parameter name "Signature".
    

Finally, the request sent to API should be:

[https://api.sunx.com/sapi/sapi/v1/trade/order?AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx&order\_id=1234567890&SignatureMethod=Ed25519&SignatureVersion=2&Timestamp=2017-05-11T15%3A19%3A30&Signature=4F65x5A2bLyMWVQj3Aqp%2BB4w%2BivaA7n5Oi2SuYtCJ9o%3D](https://api.sunx.com/sapi/sapi/v1/trade/order?AccessKeyId=e2xxxxxx-99xxxxxx-84xxxxxx-7xxxx&order_id=1234567890&SignatureMethod=Ed25519&SignatureVersion=2&Timestamp=2017-05-11T15%3A19%3A30&Signature=4F65x5A2bLyMWVQj3Aqp%2BB4w%2BivaA7n5Oi2SuYtCJ9o%3D)

For WebSocket interface:

1.  Fill the value according to required JSON schema
    
2.  The value in JSON doesn't require URL encode
    

For example:

Private channel subscription:

[PreviousInterface Type](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/interface-type)
[NextWebSocket Heartbeat](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/websocket-heartbeat)

       "SignatureMethod": "Ed25519",
       "type": "api",
       "Timestamp": "2025-09-27T11:14:48"
    }

       "Signature": "4F65x5A2bLyMWVQj3Aqp+B4w+ivaA7n5Oi2SuYtCJ9o=",
       "SignatureMethod": "HmacSHA256",

# Order Push Heartbeat | SunX

WebSocket API supports one-way heartbeat. The Server initiates ping message and the Client will return pong message. The Server sends back a heartbeat:

Copy

    {
    "op": "ping",
    "ts": "1492420473058"
    }

*   WebSocket Client should return:
    

Copy

    {
    "op": "pong",
    "ts": "1492420473058"
    }

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/websocket-heartbeat/order-push-heartbeat#note-94)

Note

*   "ts" value in the return "pong" message is the "ts" value from "ping" push Once the WebSocket Client and WebSocket Server connected, Websocket Server will send a heartbeat every 5 seconds (the frequency might change) to Wesocket Client. If WebSocket Client ignores the heartbeat message for 5 times, it will get disconnected with Websocket Sever automatically. Under abnormal conditions, WebSocket Server will return error message like:
    

Copy

    {
    "op": "pong"
    "ts": "1492420473027",
    "err-code": 2011,
    "err-msg": “detailed error message”
    }

*   Websocket Server disconnects automatically During period of building connection and authentication, Websocket Server will disconnect automatically if there is any error. The data structure before closing pushing are as below:
    

*   Server return error but remain connection After successful authentication, Server will return error but not disconnect if Client provides illegal Op or there is any internal error.
    

[PreviousMarket Heartbeat](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/websocket-heartbeat/market-heartbeat)
[NextRest](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/rest)

Last updated 2 months ago

Copy

    {
    "op": "close", // indicate Websocket Server disconnected automatically
    "ts": long // The local timestamp of Server push
    }

Copy

    {
    "op": "error", // indicate that receive illegal Op or internal error
    "ts": long// The local timestamp of Server push
    }

# Get Deposit & Withdraw records | SunX

/sapi/v1/sunperp/dw/query/deposit-withdraw

Request type: GET

Signature verification: Yes

Interface permission: Read

Rate Limit: 20 times/2s

Interface description: Parent user and sub user search for all existed withdraws and deposits and return their latest status.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/rest/wallet/get-deposit-and-withdraw-records#request-address)

Request Address

Environment

Address

Online

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

Online (preferred by aws customers)

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/rest/wallet/get-deposit-and-withdraw-records#request-parameter)

Request Parameter

Parameter

Data Type

Required

Description

Value Range

Default Value

currency

string

false

The crypto currency to withdraw or deposit

When currency is not specified, the response would include the records of ALL currencies.

type

string

true

Define transfer type to search

deposit, withdraw

deposit, withdraw, sub user can only use deposit

from

string

false

The transfer id to begin search

When 'from' is not specified, the default value would be 1 if 'direct' is 'prev' with the response in ascending order, the default value would be the ID of latest record if 'direct' is 'next' with the response in descending order.

size

string

false

The number of items to return

\[1-50\]

50

direct

string

false

the order of response

'prev' (ascending), 'next' (descending)

'next'

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/rest/wallet/get-deposit-and-withdraw-records#response-parameter)

Response Parameter

Parameter

Data Type

Required

Description

Value Range

status

string

true

Request Processing Result

error-code

string

false

Error code for withdrawal failure, only returned when the type is "withdraw" and the state is "reject", "wallet-reject" and "failed".

error-msg

string

false

Error description of withdrawal failure, only returned when the type is "withdraw" and the state is "reject", "wallet-reject" and "failed".

<data>

object

true

id

long

true

Transfer id

type

string

true

Define transfer type to search, possible values: \[deposit, withdraw\] Sub-user can only put "deposit"

currency

string

true

The crypto currency to withdraw

tx-hash

string

true

The on-chain transaction hash. If this is a "fast withdraw", then it is not on-chain transfer, and this value is empty.

chain

string

true

Block chain name

amount

float

true

The number of crypto asset transfered in its minimum unit

address

string

true

The deposit or withdraw target address

address-tag

string

true

The user defined address tag

fee

float

true

Withdrawal fee

state

string

true

deposit state

\[unknown:On-chain transfer has not been received,confirming:On-chain transfer waits for first confirmation,confirmed:On-chain transfer confirmed for at least one block, user is able to transfer and trade,safe:Multiple on-chain confirmed, user is able to withdraw,orphan:On-chain transfer confirmed but currently in an orphan branch\];withdraw state\[verifying:Awaiting verification,failed;verification failed,submitted:Withdraw request submitted successfully,reexamine:Under examination for withdraw validation,canceled:Withdraw canceled by user,pass:Withdraw validation passed,reject:Withdraw validation rejected,pre-transfer:Withdraw is about to be released,wallet-transfer:On-chain transfer initiated,wallet-reject:Transfer rejected by chain,confirmed;On-chain transfer completed with one confirmation,confirm-error:On-chain transfer faied to get confirmation,repealed:Withdraw terminated by system,risk-action-fail:Risk control verification failed,risk-action-timeout:Risk control action timeout\]

created-at

long

true

The timestamp in milliseconds for the transfer creation

updated-at

long

true

The timestamp in milliseconds for the transfer's latest update

sub-type

string

true

Deprecated parameter

request-id

string

true

Deprecated parameter

chain-full-name

string

true

Deprecated parameter

from-addr-tag

string

true

Deprecated parameter

address-id

string

true

Deprecated parameter

wallet-confirm

string

true

Deprecated parameter

</data>

true

Note：

*   Should input 'CLOUD-EXCHANGE: 6X2K9L4V1C' in the request header
    
*   API signature does not include the "/sapi/v1" part for url paths, only the "/sunx/dw/xxx" is considered.

# Ws Place  batch orders | SunX

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/websocket-trading/ws-place-batch-orders#place_batch_orders)

place\_batch\_orders

Signature verification: Yes

Interface permission: Trade

Rate Limit: Shared REST frequency limit

Interface description: This interface only supports websocket contract batch orders.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/websocket-trading/ws-place-batch-orders#subscription-address)

Subscription Address

Environment

Address

Online

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/trade

Online (preferred by aws customers)

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/trade

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/websocket-trading/ws-place-batch-orders#request-parameter)

Request Parameter

Parameter

Data Type

Required

Description

Value Range

Default Value

<data>

false

contract\_code

String

false

Symbol

margin\_mode

String

false

Margin mode: cross (Cross margin)

position\_side

String

false

Position side

long: going long; short: going short; both: One-way mode. You must input long or short and both is default.

side

String

false

Order side

buy; sell

type

String

false

Order type; enumeration

"market": market order; "limit": limit order; "post\_only": post-only order

price\_match

String

false

BBO and price are mutually exclusive

opponent: counterparty price; "optimal\_5": Best 5 BBO; "optimal\_10": Best 10 BBO; "optimal\_20": Best 20 BBO

client\_order\_id

String

false

Order ID you entered

Clients fill and maintain themselves. the value must be in \[1, 9223372036854775807\]

price

String

false

Price, applicable for limit orders only. No price input is required for market orders.

volume

String

false

Order size, specifically in Cont

reduce\_only

Integer

false

Reduce only: 0 is false; 1 is true

time\_in\_force

String

false

Enumerate FOK, IOC, and GTC. It is an optional field with GTC by default.

tp\_trigger\_price

String

false

Trigger price of your take profit order

tp\_order\_price

String

false

Price of your take profit order. (There is no need to input a price when using BBO.)

tp\_type

String

false

Type of your take profit order. "market" is default with no input. "market": market order; "limit": limit order. "optimal\_5": Best 5 BBO; "optimal\_10": Best 10 BBO; "optimal\_20": Best 20 BBO.

tp\_trigger\_price\_type

String

false

Trigger price type of your take profit order. The last price is default.

"last": last price; "market": mark price

sl\_trigger\_price

String

false

SL Trigger Price

sl\_order\_price

String

false

Price of your stop loss order. (There is no need to input a price when using BBO.)

sl\_type

String

false

Type of your stop loss order. "market" is default with no input. "market": market order; "limit": limit order. "optimal\_5": Best 5 BBO; "optimal\_10": Best 10 BBO; "optimal\_20": Best 20 BBO.

sl\_trigger\_price\_type

String

false

Trigger price type of your stop loss order. The last price is default.

"last": last price; "market": mark price

price\_protect

boolean

false

Price protection. "false" is default. The parameter is needed when you set TP/SL.

false or true

self\_match\_prevent

String

false

Self-trading prevention

Currently only supports cancel\_taker

The default is cancel\_taker

<data>

false

Notes: Notes: position\_side is the side of your position. This parameter is optional in the One-way mode. The field is optional, and only "both" can be entered. However, in Hedge mode, this field is mandatory, and only "long" or "short" can be selected. In Hedge mode, "side" and "position\_side" need to be combined. Open long (Enter "buy" in the side field; "long" in the position\_side field) Open short (Enter "sell" in the side field; "short" in the position\_side field) Close long (Enter "sell" in the side field; "long" in the position\_side field) Close short (Enter "buy" in the side field; "short" in the position\_side field) In One-way mode, a long position returns "buy," while a short position returns "sell."

# Subscribe Index Kline Data | SunX

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/websocket-subscription/public-channel/subscribe-index-kline-data#market.usdcontract_code.index.usdperiod)

market.$contract\_code.index.$period

Signature verification: Yes

Interface permission: Read

Rate Limit: For public interface to get market data such as Get Kline data, Get Market Data Overview, Get Contract Information,Get market in-depth data, Get premium index Kline, Get real-time forecast capital rate kline, Get basis data, Get the last Trade of a Contract and so on： For websocket: The rate limit for “req” request is 50 times at once. No limit for “sub” request as the data will be pushed by sever voluntarily.

Interface description: The interface supports cross margin mode and isolated margin mode.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/websocket-subscription/public-channel/subscribe-index-kline-data#subscription-address)

Subscription Address

Environment

Address

Online

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/index

Online (preferred by aws customers)

wss://api.sunx.io/ws/v1/index

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/websocket-subscription/public-channel/subscribe-index-kline-data#subscription-parameter)

Subscription Parameter

Parameter

Data Type

Required

Description

Value Range

Default Value

contract\_code

string

true

index symbol

Case-Insenstive.Both uppercase and lowercase are supported.."BTC-USDT","ETH-USDT"...

period

string

true

kline type

1min, 5min, 15min, 30min, 60min,4hour,1day, 1mon

Notes: Pushed once the index data is changed. Periodical Push when the index data hasn't changed according to the kline period.

# Market Heartbeat | SunX

WebSocket API supports two-way heartbeat. Both Server and Client can send ping message, which the opposite side can return with pong message.

*   WebSocket Server sends heartbeat：
    

`{"ping": 18212558000}`

*   WebSocket Client should respond:：
    

`{"pong": 18212558000}`

Note: Once the WebSocket Client and WebSocket Server get connected, the server will send a heartbeat every 5 seconds (the frequency might change). The connection will get disconnected automatically if the WebSocket Client ignores the heartbeat message for 5 times. The server will remain connection if the WebSocket Client responds one “ping” value within the latest 2 heartbeat messages.

[PreviousWebSocket Heartbeat](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/websocket-heartbeat)
[NextOrder Push Heartbeat](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/quick-start/websocket-heartbeat/order-push-heartbeat)

Last updated 2 months ago

---

# Get Contract Info | SunX

**/sapi/v1/public/contract\_info**

Request type: GET

Signature verification: No

Interface permission: Read

Rate Limit: For public interface used to get information of index, price limit, settlement, delivery, open positions and so on, the rate limit is 240 times every 3 second at most for each IP (this 240 times every 3 second public interface rate limit is shared by all the requests from that IP of non-marketing information, like above).

Interface description: The interface supports cross margin mode and isolated margin mode. The request parameter "support\_margin\_mode" should be "all" when querying the contract information which supports the cross margin mode and the isolated margin mode both. The value of "cross" or "isolated" just can query the contract information which only supports the cross margin mode or the isolated margin mode. Please keep attention. The request parameter "contract\_code" supports the contract code of futures, in that the format is BTC-USDT-201101; When both of pair, contract\_type and contract\_code filled in, the contract\_code is the preferred. business\_type is a required parameter when query info of futures contract, and its value must be futures or all. When support\_margin\_mode is isolated，contract\_type, business\_type should not be futures type. And when support\_margin\_mode is cross, the return data is future's data Notes：contract elements it can display more futures fields, we recommend you to use it.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/rest/basic-information/get-contract-info#request-address)

[https://api.sunx.io](https://api.sunx.io/)

# Get Futures Risk Limit | SunX

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/rest/basic-information/get-futures-risk-limit#undefined)

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/rest/basic-information/get-futures-risk-limit#sapi-v1-public-risk-limit)

/sapi/v1/public/risk/limit

Request type: GET

Signature verification: Yes

Interface permission: Read

Rate Limit: Generally, the private interface rate limit of API key is at most 144 times every 3 seconds for each UID (Trade Interface: at most 72 times every 3 seconds. Read Interface: at most 72 times every 3 seconds) (this rate limit is shared by all the altcoins contracts delivered by different date).

Interface description: Get information from the Futures Risk Limit Table.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/rest/basic-information/get-futures-risk-limit#request-address)

# Get information on swap trading fee | SunX

#### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/rest/account/get-information-on-swap-trading-fee#sapi-v1-account-fee_rate)

/sapi/v1/account/fee\_rate

Request type: POST

Signature verification: Yes

Interface permission: Read

Rate Limit: Generally, the private interface rate limit of API key is at most 144 times every 3 seconds for each UID (Trade Interface: at most 72 times every 3 seconds. Read Interface: at most 72 times every 3 seconds) (this rate limit is shared by all the altcoins contracts delivered by different date).

Interface description: The interface supports cross margin mode and isolated margin mode. The request parameter "contract\_code" supports the contract code of futures, in that the format is BTC-USDT-210625. When both of pair, contract\_type and contract\_code filled in, the contract\_code is the preferred. business\_type is a required parameter when query info of futures contract, and its value must be futures or all.

### 

[](https://sunx.gitbook.io/sunx/developer/rest/account/get-information-on-swap-trading-fee#request-address)
